======================================================================
PAGE: Flashwit
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Flashwit
======================================================================

"
[I wish] I was smart as you, Mayfly. You're so smart you got no 'pinions and that's pretty smart an' it makes me wonder if you ain't going t'waste being a heavy an' that.  A soljer.
"
―Flashwit
Flashwit
was a mean-looking
heavy
of the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
in
Sergeant
Mosel
's squad.
She was a burly,
round-faced
Napan
described as having arm muscles larger than
Fiddler
's thighs. She had cut all her hair off, and sported a bronze nose-ring. Her eyes were said to be a startlingly beautiful, emerald green.
The ground seemed to tremble when she walked.
Gesler
thought she could probably out-pull an ox and that her green eyes came from somewhere other than Napan.
She sometimes wished she was smart enough to "talk about things and all that other stuff" like
Bottle
, Gesler, and
Deadsmell
.
In
House of Chains
Flashwit's squad was part of
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
's punitive expedition against the
Army of the Apocalypse
. On the road from
Aren
to
Raraku
, the heavies had no chance to wet their swords, but Fiddler was impressed with their discipline nonetheless.
When Sergeants Fiddler and
Moak
asked her if she had heard of the legendary heavy,
Nefarias Bredd
, she claimed she heard he had killed fifty raiders.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the Army of the Apocalypse westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed.  Once the 14th Army reached the city's outskirts, Mosel and his squad decided to take revenge on the wagon whose dust they had eaten over many long miles. They bound and gagged the wagoner and the load crew in the long grass before proceeding to pry the wagon apart. Under Mosel's watchful eye, Flashwit and
Mayfly
pried the nails, studs, and fittings from the wagon's boards while
Taffo
and
Uru Hela
struggled with an axle.
While they worked, they discussed Nefarias Bredd sightings with Bottle.
Earlier, Flashwit told
Smiles
she had seen Bredd carry a dead horse into his squad's camp to roast it for meals.
Adjunct Tavore launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the heavy and
medium infantry
. Once inside the city, the Malazans immediately came under attack from swordsmen on the ground and archers in the buildings above them.  Mosel's squad of heavies waded into the swordsmen just as Fiddler launched a
cusser
from his
Crossbow
into the windows of the building above them. The resulting explosion killed
Harbyn
and Taffo, leaving only Flashwit, Mayfly, and Uru Hela. An angry Mosel descended on Fiddler before the continued fighting pulled him and his squad away.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap.  The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. At some point, Mosel was killed
and his three heavies joined a mixed group of survivors from
Cord
's, Fiddler's, and
Borduke
's squads. They fled the flames while Flashwit, Mayfly, Uru Hela, and
Shortnose
— armed only with knives and fists — defended the group against a score of fanatics.
Flashwit was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city. They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by Bottle and his
rat
.
Unlike most of the other survivors, she had not found the fires or the tunnels much to fear—instead finding the experience mostly boring.
Unaware that any had survived, the 14th Army made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
.
Faradan Sort
and
Sinn
remained behind and discovered the survivors as they crawled from the wreckage.
Captain
Sort reorganised the shattered soldiers, placing Flashwit into Gesler's Fifth squad.
After the survivors rejoined the 14th Army on the coast of the
Kokakal Sea
, Gesler and
Stormy
were given back command of the
Silanda
. Flashwit served aboard the vessel along with
Balm
and Fiddler's squads on the return voyage to
Quon Tali
.
Some festering argument between Flashwit and Shortnose led to the two wrestling on the deck, growling and biting like a pair of dogs.
The Adunct's fleet travelled to
Malaz City
where Empress
Laseen
awaited Tavore in
Mock's Hold
.  The
Silanda
joined Tavore's flagship, the
Froth Wolf
, to moor at the city pier while the rest of the fleet remained anchored in the harbour. The entire city seethed with magically induced anger against the 14th Army and the soldiers of the
Silanda
prepared to defend their ship from the mob after the Adjunct was escorted away.  Flashwit, Shortnose, Uru Hela,
Tarr
,
Corabb Bhilan Thenu'alas
, and Mayfly formed a shield wall that took the brunt of the mob's attack.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress Laseen at Malaz City and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
By this time, Flashwit was reassigned to Gesler and Stormy's squad.
Stormy happily came to think of his three female heavies as the "dread ladies", who could "stare down a rutting
bhederin
bull and beat it into a pulp".
Gesler and Fiddler's squads remained together and at first had no problem remaining hidden from enemy soldiers.
But the Letherii soon became aware of the enemy operating in their territory. Only
Corabb
's impossible luck saved them from a clever ambush in the forest when he accidentally flushed out a deer that immediately fell with twenty arrows in it. Flashwit joined Stormy and the other heavies in breaking one side of the ambush, while the other Malazans fired crossbows and sharpers at the enemy. The Malazans quickly turned the attack until the Letherii unveiled their sorcery of grey chaotic fire, killing
Sands
. Fiddler fired a cusser into the trees above the Letherii mage killing him and shredding a score of enemy soldiers before the Malazans were forced to retreat.
Gesler and Fiddler stopped their squads at an isolated farmhouse to lay a trap for a troop of mounted pursuers. While Fiddler and
Cuttle
assembled
The Drum
out of
munitions
, Gesler sent Uru Hela to investigate the occupants of the nearby farmhouse. When the heavy was only fifteen paces from the front door, an enormous
Kenryll'ah demon prince
burst out of the house to kill her with a two-handed wood-axe. Flashwit and the other heavies flanked Stormy as they charged the demon, chopping it with their swords before Gesler called the retreat.
Ironically, the demon and its fellow prince had taken up residence in the farmhouse to retire in peace. They had just wanted to be left alone and the encounter was a tragic accident.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
As the marines neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and Gesler and Fiddler's squads became separated.
A day's travel from the capital, Gesler's squad stumbled upon a village occupied by
Hellian
's squad and a number of others. Gesler and Fiddler's squad reunited at the local tavern just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village.
During the fighting, Flashwit had her helm knocked off and her head laid open, while
Bowl
was killed beside her. She was trampled by the inrushing Edur but then stood up in their midst, brandishing a
Kethra knife
in each hand.
The Edur were repelled by the arrival of
Badan Gruk
,
Sinter
, and
Primly
's fresh squads.
The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by Fist Keneb.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Gesler, Fiddler,
Urb
, and Hellian's squads were sent into the city to cause trouble while the remaining marines opened the city's west gate to Tavore's infantry. Gesler's squad soon became separated from Fiddler's after the two squads teamed to ambush an assembly of the city's Main Garrison.
After the main force of Malazans entered the city, the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
She was the object of
Shoaly
's affections.
(Information needed)
In
The Crippled God
Flashwit and
Mayfly
survived the battle with the
K'Chain Nah'ruk.
They joined
Gaunt-Eye
's 18th squad together with survivors of other squads, like
Skulldeath
and
Drawfirst
, to make up numbers.
During the march, Gaunt-Eye questioned Flashwit about Skulldeath. He was quite irritated by him and didn't believe that Skulldeath killed several K'Chain Nah'ruk
.
The 18th Squad joined the rest of the heavies and marines in the final defence of
Kaminsod's
heart.

======================================================================
PAGE: Galt
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Galt
======================================================================

Iutharal Galt
was a
medium infantryman
of the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
.  He was assigned to
Sergeant
Balm
's 9th squad.
Galt was a
Pardu
tribesman with tattooing on his face.
In
House of Chains
Galt was part of
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
's punitive expedition against the
Army of the Apocalypse
. On the road from
Aren
to
Raraku
, his squad had done their share of the fighting, and their names were well known amongst the other soldiers in the legion.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the Army of the Apocalypse westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. Upon reaching the outskirts of the city,
Corporal
Deadsmell
,
Throatslitter
, and
Widdershins
settled in for a game of
Troughs
while Galt and
Lobe
fought over dinner preparations.
Bottle
spotted the two men silently grappling over a boiling pot of water, each clutching their preferred herbs. Meanwhile, Sergeant Balm, pessimistic of their chances, went off to create his death-mask.
Adjunct Tavore launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the
Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the
heavy
and medium infantry. Once inside the city, the Malazans immediately came under attack from swordsmen on the ground and archers in the buildings above them.
Balm's squad pushed forward well beyond the other Malazan troops and took cover in a building filled with bolts of silk.  While Galt and Lobe watched the street from the windows, Deadsmell, Throatslitter, and Widdershins went to investigate a noise upstairs.  The three soldiers discovered the walls of the entire building had been filled with olive oil.  Realising what Leoman meant to do, Balm's squad attempted to report their findings to
Fist
Keneb
.  But it was too late.  When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap.  The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno.
Fleeing from the flames, they soon joined a mixed group of survivors from
Hellian
's,
Fiddler
's,
Cord
's, and
Gesler
's squads, who made their way to the Temple of the
Queen of Dreams
. Balm ordered Throatslitter to kill
Corabb Bhilan Thenu'alas
, who had also taken shelter there, but was stopped by Galt, who attempted to negotiate with his fellow Pardu.  Corabb called him a traitor.
Galt was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city.  They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by Bottle and his
rat
.
After the survivors rejoined the 14th Army on the coast of the
Kokakal Sea
, Gesler and
Stormy
were given back command of the
Silanda
. They requested that Balm and Fiddler's squads serve as their crew on the return voyage to
Quon Tali
.
The Adunct's fleet travelled to
Malaz City
where Empress
Laseen
awaited Tavore in
Mock's Hold
. The
Silanda
joined Tavore's flagship, the
Froth Wolf
, to moor at the city pier while the rest of the fleet remained anchored in the harbour.  The entire city seethed with magically induced anger against the 14th Army and the soldiers of the
Silanda
prepared to defend their ship from the mob after the Adjunct was escorted away.
Cuttle
directed Galt and Lobe to arm themselves with
sharpers
, which they used against the archers on the mob's flanks. Later, both soldiers replaced the injured
Uru Hela
and
Shortnose
in the shield wall holding the mob back. During a break in the fighting, Galt laughingly told Balm, "Our first real scrap, Sergeant. And it's against Malazans!" Balm told him to shut his mouth.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress Laseen at Malaz City and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
to invade the
Letherii Empire
.
Balm and Cord's squads took the
Silanda
to the island of
Second Maiden Fort
off the coast of Lether to establish a headquarters and resupply base for the Adjunct.
They found the island on the verge of being destroyed under a mountain of ice released by the collapse of
Gothos
' ancient
Omtose Phellack
ritual, but
Sinn
was able to hold the ice back with her magic until its force was spent. The island's self-declared ruler,
Brullyg
, gratefully welcomed the Malazans as royal guests until they placed him under house arrest and secretly took control of the island.
Balm's squad kept Brullyg under guard and monitored the island from its only town, as Cord's squad patrolled the island's coast and interior while awaiting Tavore's arrival.
Galt and Lobe guarded Brullyg in his rooms with
Masan Gilani
, who was on loan from
Urb
's squad, while Balm, Deadsmell, and Throatslitter spent their days in
Harridict Tavern
observing the clientele. All three of Brullyg's guards served as muscle, but the voluptuous Gilani also kept Brullyg stupid and docile. Galt and Lobe killed time playing games of
Troughs
. When
Shurq Elalle
and
Skorgen Kaban
managed to gain an audience with Brullyg, Galt took the lead in handling the visitors while Lobe readied his crossbow and Gilani held a knife to Brullyg's back. After taking the two pirates prisoner, Galt dropped his act of badly spoken Letherii.
Meanwhile Tavore sent Fist Keneb's marines to the mainland, spreading them in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast and burning their
transport vessels
behind them. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Shortly after Adjunct Tavore arrived at the island with the rest of the Malazan fleet,
Yan Tovis
and the other
Shake
came to stake their claim to the island. Galt had to draw his sword to restrain
Yedan Derryg
from throwing Brullyg, the Shake pretender, out a window at Yan Tovis' command. Once Brullyg's safety was assured, Tavore she hired Shurq Elalle to guide them to the mouth of the
Lether River
leading to Letheras.
Balm and Cord's squads made the journey on the
Silanda
.
The Adjunct's fleet made landfall near Letheras in time to see a massive release of enemy sorcery near Fist Keneb's reported position. Believing the marines had been wiped out, Tavore's forces defeated the city's
Imperial Brigade
.
Balm's squad, along with Masan Gilani, secured horses to chase down fleeing Letherii soldiers and continued further inland towards the city. When they arrived at the field where
Beak
had saved Keneb's marines, they were mystified to find no bodies.
Approaching the city's western gate, they found it in control of Keneb's troops. By this time, "the Confusion" had come upon Balm and he was incapable of communicating with anyone. Deadsmell assured Keneb the sergeant would snap out of it soon, as Masan Gilani raced back to fetch reinforcements from Tavore.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
He did not survive the exchange with the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
.

Gill Slime
was a
mage
in the regular infantry of the
Bonehunters
. Gill used Illusionary magic.
In
The Crippled God
Gill along with a group of other regulars rushed out to defend
the Adjunct's
position in the battle against the
Forkrul Assail
. Gill and fellow mage
Asp Slither
were detailed by
Sergeant
Ordinary Grey
to find the commander of the opposing force and hit the person with full force.
They used illusions to take out the
Kolansii
commander then, having exhausted magic, joined in the regular fighting.

Grid Ffan
was a
Falari
in the Third Squad, Eleventh Company of the
Bonehunters
.
In
The Crippled God
On the last day before
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
sacrificed her blood for water in the

, Grid Ffan had carried
Sample
on his back. The only thing that had kept them both alive was their love for one another.

Forkrul Assail
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Gripe
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Gripe
======================================================================

Gripe
was a
sergeant
in the
Malaz 14th Army
, likely in the
8th Legion
's 9th Company.
Beak
was a
mage
in the Gripe's squad.
In
Reaper's Gale
During the initial stage of the
Bonehunters
' invasion of the
Letherii Empire
,
Fist
Keneb
entrusted
Captain
Faradan Sort
with keeping in communication with the individual
Marine
squads spread across the countryside. She chose Beak from Gripe's squad to serve as her second in this task. She said none in the squad liked the mage and would not rue his loss.
Trivia
In a 2021 interview, author
Steven Erikson
laughed when referring to Gripe. "I don't think [Sergeant Gripe] is mentioned ever [again], which is a shame because it's such a great name. I wish I'd gone to Sergeant Gripe a few times. I love that name."

======================================================================
PAGE: Grub
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Grub
======================================================================

Grub
was the adopted name of an orphan boy adopted
by
Captain Keneb
from among the survivors of the
Chain of Dogs
.
He was placed in Keneb's care by another survivor,
Duiker
, the Imperial Historian,
and raised by Keneb in the company of the
Malaz 14th Army
.
He was a toddler with a tangled shock of blond hair and a deeply tanned, cherubic face.
His face was often smeared with dirt.
Grub was unaccountably attuned to the mystical aspects of the world, though he had not been trained as a
mage
.
In
House of Chains
Grub first appeared as a dire omen before
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
and the
8th Legion
in
Aren
as the Malaz 14th Army readied to march against the
Army of the Whirlwind
in
Raraku
.  As the Adjunct reviewed her troops, the boy slipped the supervision of his nurse to stand in Tavore's footsteps carrying a human bone in his hand.  The troops were shocked into silence.
"
There was no doubt among them concerning the meaning of the omen, and Strings was inclined to agree. A child leads us to our deaths. A leg bone to signify our march, withered under the curse of the desert sun. We've all lived too long, seen too much, to deceive ourselves of this one brutal truth: this army of recruits now see themselves as already dead.
"
―Strings explains the Legion's reaction
It was up to
Fiddler
and the other veterans to turn the omen to their advantage by making the bones a symbol of the army and a portion of their uniforms.
By the time the army reached the Whirlwind encircling Raraku,
Fist
Gamet
had decided to end his life for fatal mistakes made during an engagement against
Leoman
's desert warriors.  Before he could walk into the Whirlwind's fury, he was unaccountably intercepted by Grub.  The child told Gamet that he spent too much time thinking about things there was no point in thinking about.  Then he said Keneb was looking for Gamet and went to tell his father he found him.  When Keneb found Gamet soon after, Keneb told the Fist he had not seen the boy and had never heard him speak before.
Gamet saw Grub again on the eve of the
Battle of Raraku
.  The boy woke
Nil
and
Nether
to observe the spirits of the dead gathering on the battlefield.  Then the boy told Gamet to join the cavalry forming on the battlefield's centre.
After Gamet and the spirits of the dead attacked and destroyed the opposing
Dogslayers
, it was revealed that Gamet had died in his sleep back in camp.
According to the Epigraph for Chapter 19 in
House of Chains
, Grub eventually became the
First Sword
of the Late Empire period.
"
It was said the captain's adopted child - who at that time was known by the unfortunate name of Grub - refused the wagon on the march. That he walked the entire way, even as, in the first week beneath the year's hottest sun, fit and hale soldiers stumbled and fell.
This is perhaps invention, for by all accounts he was at that time no more than five years of age. And the captain himself, from whose journals much of that journey and the clash in which it culminated is related in detail, writes very little of Grub, more concerned as he was with the rigours of command. As a result, of the future First Sword of the Late Empire period, scant details, beyond the legendary and probably fictitious, are known.
"
―Lives of the Three
Moragalle
In
The Bonehunters
Sinn
was frequently found accompanying him. He was also accompanied by the
Hengese
lap dog,
Roach
, and
Wickan cattle-dog
,
Bent
.  Sinn, whom many assumed to be either mute or dumb, did speak to Grub, however, normally only when out of earshot of others.
Adjunct Tavore Paran used Grub as a messenger to call impromptu staff meetings.
When
Quick Ben
spoke the boy's name he made a warding gesture and indicated to Fiddler that there was more to Grub than he appeared.
A few days after the 14th Army had been resupplied with troops, Grub gave Keneb some of his cryptic answers, amongst them saying that 'she is our last hope' but not naming 'she'.
Keneb thought of Grub's comments as a 'disordered host of peculiar observations'. Amongst those observations, Grub seemed to hint at glory or maybe infamy to come for
Temul
, in whose company the boy was often found.
When Sinn managed to make a firebreak for the soldiers trapped in
Y'Ghatan
, Grub told the Adjunct exactly how many were coming through, even as they appeared in the distance.
After the fall of Y'Ghatan, Grub again gave Keneb cryptic clues, seemingly displaying knowledge of the soldiers tunneling beneath the city as well as other things to come.
Grub told Keneb to delay the boarding of the ships by one day as otherwise they would all die two days after leaving the
Sepik Island
. Amongst other things, Grub also said that he found a bone whistle and would keep it for him who would want it back.
Keneb admitted to Tavore that he caused the delay on Grub's advice just as the survivors who tunneled their way out of Y'Ghatan arrived down the road.
Grub appeared towards the end, during the clash in
Malaz City
, to inform
Lostara
that she was needed.
He led her to
Pearl
who was by then suffering a long drawn-out death, and persuaded her to kill him out of mercy, whilst at the same time, judiciously not telling her who killed Pearl, so that she would not seek revenge.
Grub then led her to watch as the
Eres'al
left the body of the dead
T'amber
, telling Lostara that she must never tell Tavore about this and agreeing that this and the secret about Tavore's
sister
were the only ones which she had to keep. He then asked her to join the Bonehunters and help Tavore.
In
Reaper's Gale
The Bonehunters followed the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that ravaged
Sepik
across the sea back to
Lether
to invade the
Letherii Empire
. The army would have quickly dissolved without funds to pay the soldiers, but Grub somehow learned that
Banaschar
held the accumulated stolen wealth of
D'rek
's faithful and passed the information on to Lostara Yil. Grub spent much of the ocean voyage climbing the rigging of the
Froth Wolf
with his
Nacht
companions,
Mape
,
Pule
, and
Rind
, with whom he was able to communicate in someway.
He informed Lostara Yil that "the world is drowning."
Fist Keneb's
marines
were spread in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Keneb followed in their wake with six squads of marines, while
Faradan Sort
and
Beak
attempted to keep lines of communication open between both groups.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the
Malazan
invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
Instead the marines saw intense action, and as they neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and their munition supplies dwindled.
The Malazan fleet bearing the Adjunct and the Bonehunters' main force sailed up the
Lether River
towards Letheras.
Some among the Bonehunters thought Keneb's troops had been sent to their doom,
and their fears seemed to be proved true. As they made landfall outside the city, those on the fleet saw a massive release of enemy sorcery near Fist Keneb's reported position near the city walls. Grub watched with Sinn on the
Froth Wolf's
foredeck, and begun dancing about the deck talking of candles. Lostara Yil thought him addled, but Adjunct Tavore had confidence that "Grub does not behave like a child who has lost a father."
Somehow Grub knew of Beak's sacrifice that had saved Fist Keneb and his soldiers.
The Bonehunters defeated the Letherii
Imperial Brigade
and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
He and Sinn followed Bent and Roach into the dying
Azath Tower
in
Letheras
and disappeared into a
Warren
for a time, only to reappear at a crucial point in the battle between the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
and the
K'Chain Che'Malle
. Their intervention turned the battle in favour of the K'Chain Che'Malle.
In
The Crippled God
Whilst riding with the K'Chain Che'Malle towards the Bonehunters, Grub asked Sinn to reach out with her mind to the Adjunct. Sinn told him that the barrier of the
Otataral
sword would not let 'them' in. This seemed to indicate that at this point Grub was able to use magic intentionally.
He finally parted company with Sinn and ultimately took command of the Letherii troops in battle against the
Kolansii
.
Speculations
It has been speculated that Grub's three friends from Fiddler's Deck of Dragons reading in
The Bonehunters
were the three Nachts: Mape, Pule, and Rind.

PAGE: Guano
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Guano
======================================================================

Guano
was a member of
Sergeant
Moak
's
Medium infantry
squad of the 9th Company,
8th Legion
in the
Malaz 14th Army
.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. Upon reaching the outskirts of the city, Moak prepared a stew for his squad using a ripened fish he had carried for weeks.  When his squad all "got the squats", he blamed it on their weak stomachs while a true soldier like himself suffered only from belches that smelled of rotting fish guts.
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the
heavy
and medium infantry. Barely a street in and fearing an ambush, Sergeant
Gesler
called up Moak's squad as well as
Thom Tissy
's sappers and
Tugg
's heavies to clear the surrounding buildings. In the fighting that followed, the poorly trained sappers misfired their
munitions
. One shrieking sapper exited the building fully aflame.  As Moak's squad went to help him, the sapper's munitions satchel went off killing Guano and Moak's entire squad.

======================================================================
PAGE: Gullstream
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Gullstream
======================================================================

Gullstream
was a crossbowman and member of the
Ehrlitan Guard
.
He had a high forehead that was alternately described as covered with prominent white blotches
or disfigured by a piebald blotch of pink.
He had almond-shaped eyes and was dark-skinned. According to
Smiles
, there was "something about Gullstream that made women take a second and third look". She also suspected that he had
Tiste Andii
blood.
He had the habit of wiping his runny nose on the sleeve of his uniform.
In
House of Chains
Gullstream was present when
Karsa Orlong
was arrested in
Ehrlitan
and brought to the imperial prison with his erstwhile slavers
Silgar
and
Damisk
.  Gullstream and
Jibb
served as Karsa's guards.
In
Reaper's Gale
Gullstream later joined
Sergeant
Thom Tissy
's 12th Squad of the
8th Legion
, 9th Company of the
Bonehunters
, along with
Corporal
Tulip
,
Ramp
,
Bellig Harn
, Jibb, and
Mudslinger
. He served as
Medium infantry
.
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Fist
Keneb
followed in their wake with six squads of marines, including Tissy's 12th squad.
Once the marines began engaging with the enemy, Keneb had difficulty maintaining contact with his lead elements. Tissy told Keneb that he and the others in the squad understood his anxiety at following impossible orders under difficult conditions. The Fist called him presumptuous and told him to tell his squad to stop theorising.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
As the marines neared Letheras fighting became more desperate, and a large force of Edur stood between Keneb's troops and the forward marines. Thom Tissy heartened the Fist by claiming his troops were ready for a hard fight. They fought their way to a village where all the remaining squads had converged before continuing on together to the capital.
Thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing them towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Thom Tissy's squad was among those sent to secure the city's western gate from the inside to allow the main army entrance into the city. City Garrison soldiers tried to retake the gate in bloody fighting, but Tissy's squad held on long enough for
Balm
's squad, and then others, to arrive.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
(Information needed)

======================================================================
PAGE: Gupp
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Gupp
======================================================================

Gupp
was a soldier with the
Medium infantry
of the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
, a member of the 12th squad under
Sergeant
Thom Tissy
.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed.
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's sappers to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. The sappers were organised into groups with each group protected by a
mage
. Gupp took on the role of sapper for the first time ever that night, and his group included
Able
,
Bowl
,
Jump
, and
Taffo
with
Balgrid
as their mage.
Once the walls were breached Gupp quickly returned to Thom Tissy's squad of medium infantry.
First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the
heavy
and medium infantry.
Barely a street in and fearing an ambush, Sergeant
Gesler
ordered some of the freshly-made sappers from Tissy's squad, Gupp amongst them, to clear some of the buildings ahead. Gupp, Able, and Jump, instead of throwing their
sharpers
, went inside a building to set them off. Gesler heard the sharpers then thought he saw the flames of a
Burner
. One of the three soldiers stumbled out, wreathed in flames and was shot by Gesler but too late to save those of
Moak
's squad running to help the man. They were all killed when his munitions pouch exploded. The building was engulfed in flames and the other two presumably perished in the flames inside. It is unknown if Gupp was the soldier who had stumbled outside or one of the two who perished inside the building.

PAGE: Hanfeno
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters

======================================================================

Hanfeno
was a
heavy
in the
Malaz 14th Army
. Circumstantial evidence suggests he was in the 3rd Company of the
8th Legion
under
Captain Kindly
. He was often in the company of
Senny
.
Kindly thought him thick and pigheaded.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
, the 14th Army marched to the coast of the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and return to
Quon Tali
.  While waiting for their squad's turn to board, Hanfeno and Senny gathered hundreds of bird bones to turn into fetishes for their fellow
Bonehunters
.  Hanfeno drilled holes in the bones for easier attachment to the soldiers' uniforms.
Nok's ships were later met off the coast of
The Horn
by the
Jakatakan Fleet
and ordered to
Malaz City
. Hanfeno and Senny were amongst those giving Commander
Exent Hadar
and his ships a 'defecating' send-off when the two fleets parted.  Captain Kindly ordered Pores to put the two on report.
At Malaz City, Kindly's troops remained on their ships in the harbour while
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
went ashore to meet Empress
Laseen
in
Mock's Hold
.  Fighting broke out on the pier between the citizens of Malaz City and the 14th soldiers guarding the Adjunct's
flagship
.  Kindly rejected Pores' request to send aid, saying he would be happy to promote Hanfeno in the Lieutenant's place while Senny took bets on whether Pores could survive swimming to shore across the shark-filled harbour.

======================================================================
PAGE: Hanno
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Hanno
======================================================================

Hanno
was a
heavy
in
Sergeant
Sobelone
's squad in the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed.  Hanno married fellow soldier,
Shortnose
, about one week before reaching the city.  According to
Corporal
Reem
, it "aint his face she adores, if you know what I mean."
Once the 14th Army reached the city's outskirts, an impromptu wrestling match broke out between Shortnose and
Saltlick
after Saltlick bit Shortnose's ear off. The rest of Sobelone and
Tugg
's squads gathered around the two straining men, watching and placing bets. Hanno bet against her husband.
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the heavy and
medium infantry
.  Once inside the city, the Malazans immediately came under attack from hidden archers and warriors. Sobelone and
Toles
were killed in one such ambush. Hanno and the survivors of Sobelone's squad were rallied by Sergeant
Hellian
, who orchestrated a counterattack against their ambushers using
smokers
.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap.  The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. Hanno's and Hellian's squads joined a mixed group of survivors from
Cord
's,
Fiddler
's, and
Borduke
's squads fleeing the flames to the Temple of the
Queen of Dreams
. Hanno was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city.  They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
.
Having lost most of her squad, she was afterwards reassigned to
Urb
's 13th squad of the
Bonehunters
.
Hanno and the other survivors eventually caught up to the 14th Army west of
Sotka
as it embarked on
Admiral
Nok
's Malazan Imperial Fleet to return to
Quon Tali
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Urb and Hellian's squads remained together.
After defeating a troop of mounted Edur soldiers at
Boaral Keep
, Hellian put the squads on horseback and determined to rush ahead for
Letheras
, working from tavern to tavern along the way.
They ambushed sixteen Letherii and four Edur mounted on horseback, slaying the Edur with
Crossbow
bolts to the head and hitting either end of the Letherii column with
sharpers
. The Letherii veterans recovered more quickly than expected and Hanno had her skull cleaved by a Letherii sword. Urb pulled Hanno's killer from his saddle and struck him with his mailed fist, punching the man's teeth into the back of his skull.
Presumably, Shortnose learned of his wife's death when his squad later united with Urb's at a village a day's travel from Letheras.

Corporal
Harbyn
was a
heavy
in the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
.
Harbyn was a member of
Sergeant
Mosel
's Squad.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. During the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
, the city's walls were breached by
Sappers
.  First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the heavies.  The marines were immediately ambushed by swordsmen on the ground and archers in the buildings above them.  Mosel's squad of heavies waded into the swordsmen just as
Fiddler
launched a
cusser
from his
Crossbow
into the windows of the building above them.  The resulting explosion tore away Harbyn's lower half, killing him instantly. An angry Mosel descended on Fiddler before the continued fighting pulled him away.

PAGE: Hare Ravage
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Hare_Ravage
======================================================================

Hare Ravage was a soldier in the regular infantry of the
Bonehunters
. He was
Kanese
and was described as his squad's huge mailed fist.
He was the author of the poem
Adjunct
.
In
The Crippled God
Ravage, along with about ten others, rushed out to defend
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
's position in the battle against the
Forkrul Assail
. He fought alongside
Ruthan Gudd
in defending the retreat of the Adjunct back to the main force, matching the ferocity of Gudd's attacks. When relief forces arrived, he cooled his forehead against Gudd's ice-sheathed side.
Poetry
"
Well enough she faces away
Walking past these dripping thrones
No one knows where the next foot
Falls
When we stumble in the shadows
Our standards bow to wizened winds
I saw that look beneath the rim
Of blistered iron
And it howled to the men kneeling
In the square and the dog sleeps on
In the cool foot of the wall, no fools there
She was ever looking elsewhere
Like a disenchanted damsel
A shift of her shoulder
Sprawls corpses into her wake
No matter
There was a child dream once
You remember well
Was she the mother or did that tit
Seep seduction?
All these thrones I built with my own
Hands
Labours of love thin over ragged nails
I wanted benediction, or the slip away
Of clothes, whichever bends my way
Behind her back
Oh we were guards then, stern sentinels
And these grilled masks smelling of blood
Now sweat something old
We never knew what we were guarding
We never do and never will
But I swear to you all:
I will die at its feet before I take a step inside
Call me duty and be done with it
Or roll from your tongue that sweet curl
That is valour
While the dogs twitch in dream
Like children left lying
Underfoot
"
―
Adjunct
Hare Ravage

======================================================================
PAGE: Hellian
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Hellian
======================================================================

Hellian
Biographical information
Race
Human
(
Kartoolian
)
Gender
Female
Social information
Affiliation
Malazan Empire
Bonehunters
Occupation(s)
Soldier
Rank
Sergeant
Hellian
was a nineteen-year-old
sergeant
of the city guard in the
Septarch District
of the city of
Kartool
.
She harboured a deep and abiding phobia about spiders and as there were plenty of them in Kartool, maintained a more or less permanent state of inebriation to avoid going into hysterics over them. Upon first meeting her,
Banaschar
inferred to her that the lack of sobriety was probably the reason she had not been promoted to the vacant rank of
captain
in her district.
She was described as a soft-featured woman with bright always wet lips.
In
The Bonehunters
Hellian was called by Banaschar to investigate trouble at the Grand Temple of
D'rek
in Kartool. Upon breaking down the doors, they found everyone inside slaughtered. Banaschar then disappeared, leaving Hellian to predict to her
corporal
,
Urb
, that they would be in trouble over this and be sent off to some trouble spot.
Hellian was proved correct and found herself and the other witnesses transferred far away to the
Malaz 14th Army
,
via
Malaz City
, then
Nap
and
Unta
. They joined up with the 14th when the army was resupplied with troops on the way to
Y'Ghatan
.
Her undersized squad consisted of only Urb,
Brethless
, and
Touchy
.
Hellian kept her squad bivouacked by the rum wagon, but
Cuttle
commented that she never seemed so drunk she could not keep her eyes open and that she had a capable corporal.
Hellian was one of the group of soldiers who survived the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by escaping through tunneling their way out from under the city.
As she would not go underground due to her fear of spiders, her corporal Urb knocked her out and carried her into the tunnel.
By the time they escaped the smoldering ruins, the 14th Army had made its way to the coast of the
Kokakal Sea
to be removed to safety by
Admiral
Nok
's fleet ahead of the
plague
spreading through Seven Cities. Hellian and the other Y'Ghatan survivors caught up to the 14th Army in time to join them.
The Malazan fleet brought the 14th Army to Malaz City where Empress
Laseen
waited to meet the Adjunct in
Mock's Hold
. Tavore ordered all but her escort ships to remain anchored in the harbour, but Hellian was so desperate for a drink that she jumped overboard fully armoured intending to swim to the docks. Touchy and Brethless were startled, but decided it was better she drown than they get in trouble for alerting anyone.
Amidst the crowds, she was enraged to spot Banaschar, the priest who had ruined her life at Kartool and set her on the path into the army. She angrily dispatched
Saygen Maral
, the
Claw
assassin attempting to kill Banaschar, claiming the priest was hers to put under arrest. Then she dragged the priest past the city's violent mobs into
Smiley's
to answer questions and buy her a drink.
The two eventually exited
Smiley's
in a drunken stupor just as
Fiddler
,
Gesler
, and
Stormy
passed on the street outside with
Legana Breed
. The 14th Army officers safely brought them back through the angry mobs on the waterfront to the 14th Army's ships.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress Laseen at Malaz City and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Fist
Keneb
followed in their wake with six squads of marines, while Captain
Faradan Sort
and
Beak
attempted to keep lines of communication open between both groups.
Hellian was put in charge of the newly reorganised 8th squad.
In her constant inebriated state she came to believe Touchy and Brethless were a single four-armed corporal named "Touchy Brethless".
Others like
Maybe
she had trouble remembering because of their "stupid" names.
Touchy
, corporal #1
Brethless
, corporal #2
Balgrid
, squad mage
Tavos Pond
, marine
Maybe
, sapper
Lutes
, squad healer
Hellian's squad was paired with Urb's for the landings. When they assembled on the beach, Urb found her arranging casks of rum she had salvaged from the burning ships amongst her squad.
The two squads remained together and Bowl and
Balgrid
used magic to cover their tracks.
In their first action, they defeated a troop of Edur at
Boaral Keep
where
Lutes
had rested his crossbow on her back to fire as she vomited. They acquired the Edur's mounts at Hellian's suggestion and pushed hard inland for the capital, fighting from tavern to tavern.
The two squads began taking trophies of ears and fingers and tying them to their belts.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
When the two squads ambushed a mixed mounted troop of Letherii and Edur, the Letherii veterans recovered more quickly than expected and killed
Hanno
--the Malazans' first casualty.
In the aftermath, an inebriated Hellian tried to bed a terrified Urb before being interrupted by the arrival of Faradan Sort and Beak. Hellian and Urb's mounted squads were well ahead of the others. Sort approved, but asked them to pace themselves while she got the other marines on horseback.
Hellian and other Bonehunters occupying a bar during the invasion of Lether - Interpretation by
Shadaan
As the marines neared Letheras fighting became more desperate, although Hellian earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, moneylenders, and debt-holders in each village. Then they stayed in the village tavern--decorated with the severed heads of their victims--until it was dry before moving on to the next.
Fiddler and Gesler's squads found them drinking and singing at a tavern a day's travel from the capital. Fiddler did not approve, but could not argue with Hellian's success where all the other squads had failed miserably.
Almost as soon as the marines were reunited, a force of hundreds of Edur enveloped the village.
During the fighting, Urb was an exhausted nervous wreck just trying to keep Hellian alive as she had somehow traded her shield for the lid of an ale cask. An Edur lance pinned his side as he tried to protect her. Only the healing magic of
Mulvan Dreader
saved his life.
The Edur were repelled by the arrival of
Badan Gruk
,
Sinter
, and
Primly
's fresh squads.
The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by Fist Keneb.
While they waited, Hellian became the object of
Skulldeath
's affection after drunkenly announcing that she was the "Queen of Kartool".
The notoriously celibate soldier, and last in his family line, was saving his seed for a woman of royalty.
From then on he was besotted with her, announcing he had given his heart to her and following her everywhere.
Hellian returned the favour, forcing Primly to step in and pry them apart.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under Beak's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white.
(Hellian had passed out during the event and awoke to think everyone was pulling an elaborate trick on her by bleaching their hair, but left her empty flask on Beak's barrow).
The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Hellian, Urb, Fiddler, and Gesler's squads were sent into the city to cause trouble while the remaining marines opened the city's west gate to Tavore's infantry. Hellian's squad quickly disappeared into a local tavern and Urb was tasked with finding them.
He found her threatening to hang a
Letherii barkeep
unless he revealed the tavern's hidden stock.
After the main force of Malazans entered the city, the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
Over the course of the Malazan series, Hellian developed a reputation as a sergeant whose troops survived battle.
In
Dust of Dreams
(Information needed)
In
The Crippled God
During the final battle of the Malazan
marines
and
Hedge's
Bridgeburners
at which they defended the
Crippled God
, Urb at last confessed his love for Hellian,
to which she responded enthusiastically.
Both Hellian and Urb were amongst those who survived the battle.
Trivia
Steven Erikson
says he remembers "getting some pushback on the Hellian character from somebody saying...alcoholism is not that nice, etc., etc. Well, my father was an alcoholic. So I grew up in the family of that, so I reject that kind of pushback. It's more a case of this is fiction and we can actually have a laugh. You know, ultimately, laughter is pretty healthy and I often go in that direction at unexpected times. And certainly with Hellian, yeah, there's something profoundly tragic to the character, but she's also extremely comedic, inadvertently so, and I'm not gonna shy away from that and go all heavy on everybody. There's places for that and she's not one of them."

Corporal Nobbs

Coalhands

Shadaan

Shadaan

Jason Dement

======================================================================
PAGE: Himble Thrup
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Himble_Thrup
======================================================================

Himble Thrup
was a short, round-faced but scrawny soldier in the
Bonehunters
. His eyes were described as watery.
Pores
thought of Himble as an old man.
In
The Crippled God
Himble had formerly been a
Heavy
but in the engagement with the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
the fingers of both his hands had been chopped off clean at the knuckles. The shield side hand had been wounded during the first stand and the sword one in the fourth push. Himble was forced out of the heavies, presumably because he was no longer capable of functioning as one, and ended up as a clerk for Lieutenant 'Master Sergeant Quartermaster' Pores as he was still able to write, having retained both of his thumbs.
According to
Shortnose
, Himble had done a lot of damage to the Nah'ruk during that fight.
Himble was ranked
Corporal
and proved to be a very efficient clerk. When Pores dictated a lengthy, detailed missive and asked Himble to read back what he had written, the clerk had condensed it to one sentence with which Pores was happy. Later however, delivering the tablet and finding the wax melted, he then recounted the original lengthy message verbatim.
His disfigurement led to him being given the new name of
Shorthand
, which he actually preferred to Himble Thrup.
Fist
Blistig
had ordered Lieutenant 'Quartermaster'
Pores
to secretly reserve a number of barrels of water specifically for his own personal use.
When water had become sparse, Himble, who was guarding the wagon the barrels were supposed to be on, was knocked out by Blistig's man
Rackle
, who hit him in the side of the head with a mace, whilst the Fist stabbed Pores intending to kill him in order to obtain 'his' water barrels and to hide the truth. Himble's body was then dragged to one side by
Stull
and
Bester
.
He was found some time later with the life-threatening injury of a broken skull.
Pores later reminisced on having nursed Himble after he himself had lain half-dead for several days, spoon-feeding the old man who was just staring into space, waiting for him to say at least one word.
From Pores' reminiscing it is clear that Himble survived for at least a few days, however, no further reference was made to him.

======================================================================
PAGE: Hobble (Sub-Fist)
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Hobble_(Sub-Fist)
======================================================================

Hobble (Sub-Fist)
and
Kellant
were
Sub-Fists
under
Fist
Keneb
.
In
Dust of Dreams
As the
Bonehunters
travelled eastward across the
Lether
continent, Fist Keneb was concerned that he was becoming far too reliant on both Sub-Fist Hobble and Sub-Fist Kellant for assistance with logistical aspects of what should have been
his
responsibility as Fist. Hobble and Kellant, Keneb recognized, were veteran officers and experienced campaigners, but they had more than enough demands upon their time and energy as it was - with each commanding 'regulars', "foot, skirmishers, scouts and archers". The two Sub-Fists probably had little good to say about him, Keneb felt.

======================================================================
PAGE: Honey
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Honey
======================================================================

Honey
was a
sapper
in
Pravalak Rim
's 4th squad,
8th Legion
, 3rd Company in the
Bonehunters
. He had a history of directing his unwanted affections towards the female soldiers around him. His current object of affection was
Skim
, although he also had his eye on
Kisswhere
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the
marines
in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Sinter's squad, along with
Badan Gruk
's 5th and
Primly
's 10th squads, landed furthest south of all the marines. Remaining together, they saw little resistance moving east and soon reached a river. Rather than slog through through waist-deep swamp muck, they stole a fisher boat and sailed upriver. They made excellent time until running into a Letherii galley in the night. Kisswhere and Sinter were lost in the water during a discharge of
Moranth munitions
. Forced ashore, they were pursued day and night, using up their mages dodging and ducking enemy attacks.
Corporal
Pravalak Rim
led the 4th squad in Sinter's place and Honey inherited Kisswhere's collection of
sharpers
.
Brushing off Honey's advances and warning him to stop addressing her as "beloved", Skim facetiously blamed him for Kisswhere's death, claiming Kisswhere had blown up her sister and herself to get away from him. Then Skim tormented
Nep Furrow
asking him to bless (or curse) her own sharpers in the same manner he had done for Kisswhere before her death. Death was the only way Honey would leave her alone. Nep Furrow wanted nothing to do with the "teasin' tit-woman."
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the
Malazan
invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
The marines further north saw intense action, and as they neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and their munition supplies dwindled.
Hellian
and
Urb
's squads earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler
and
Gesler
's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
Three days after leaving the river, Sinter, Primly, and Badan Gruk's squads came upon the overwhelmed Malazans and turned the tide of battle with their fresh supply of munitions. The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by
Fist
Keneb
.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, the seized the city's western gate to allow the rest of the army entrance.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.

PAGE: Hubb
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters

======================================================================

Corporal
Hubb
was part of
Borduke
's 6th squad of the
8th Legion
's 9th Company in the
Malaz 14th Army
out of
Aren
.
In
House of Chains
Hubb was part of
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
's punitive expedition against the
Army of the Apocalypse
.  On the road to
Raraku
, Hubb was present at the 9th Company
Scorpion
fight, and was likely the Holder for his squad's entrant.
When
Leoman
and his two hundred desert warriors launched a surprise pre-dawn attack on the Malazan camp, Borduke's squad grabbed their
Crossbows
and prepared to fire on the warriors as they rode past their tents.
Maybe
fired early, spoiling his squad's attack and allowing
Corabb
to make a spectacular escape.  Hubb commented that Corabb's horse might have killed their cook.  To which Borduke replied that the gods were smiling down on them.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
, Leoman led the Army of the Apocalypse westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed.  In the hours before battle,
Maybe
's talk of the dangers and bloody effects of misfired
Moranth Mountains
sent
Lutes
vomiting and the other members of Borduke's squad experienced "sympathetic heaves".  Borduke stormed off in disgust.
During the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
, Hubb's squad was initially short its two
mages
,
Balgrid
and
Tavos Pond
, as well as Maybe, its
sapper
.  But after the three had assisted in breaching the city's walls, they quickly rejoined his squad and Borduke's soldiers were first into the breach.  But just as they cleared the wall's rubble, they were ambushed by archers and swordsmen.  Hubb immediately took an arrow to the gut and curled up on the ground. Borduke and
Ibb
died in the same attack.
Trivia
During the scorpion fights it was implied that Hubb was the Holder for
Clawmaster
.  But Hubb was in Borduke's squad, whose scorpion was
Mangonel
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Hunt
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters, Humans
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Hunt
======================================================================

Hunt
was the
corporal
in
Primly
's 10th squad,
8th Legion
, 3rd Company of the
Bonehunters
. He was from
Kartool
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the
marines
in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Primly's squad, along with
Sinter
's 4th and
Badan Gruk
's 5th squads, landed furthest south of all the marines. Remaining together, they saw little resistance moving east and soon reached a river. Rather than slog through through waist-deep swamp muck, they stole a fisher boat and sailed upriver. They made excellent time until running into a Letherii galley in the night.
Kisswhere
and Sinter were lost in the water during a discharge of
Moranth munitions
. Forced ashore, they were pursued day and night, using up their mages dodging and ducking enemy attacks. Somewhere along the way
Masker
was also lost, leaving Primly with only one heavy.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the
Malazan
invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
The marines further north saw intense action, and as they neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and their munition supplies dwindled.
Hellian
and
Urb
's squads earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler
and
Gesler
's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
Three days after leaving the river, Primly, Sinter, and Badan Gruk's squads came upon the overwhelmed Malazans. Badan Gruk immediately thought to pass around them, but Hunt snorted in disgust before he and Primly argued that their squads were ready to fight. The three squads turned the tide of battle with their fresh supply of munitions. The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by
Fist
Keneb
.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, the seized the city's western gate to allow the rest of the army entrance.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
(Information needed)
In
The Crippled God
It was revealed he had died in the battle against the
Nah'ruk
at the end of
Dust of Dreams
.

Ibb
was one of
Borduke
's 6th squad
marines
in the
8th Legion
's 9th Company of the
Malaz 14th Army
.
In
House of Chains
Ibb was part of
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
's punitive expedition against the
Army of the Apocalypse
. He served as the colour commentator on the
scorpion
fights between the squads cooked up by
Fiddler
and
Cuttle
.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the Army of the Apocalypse westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed.  In the hours before battle,
Maybe
's talk of the dangers and bloody effects of misfired
Moranth Mountains
sent
Lutes
vomiting and the other members of Borduke's squad experienced "sympathetic heaves".  Borduke stormed off in disgust.

======================================================================
PAGE: Jamber Bole
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Jamber_Bole
======================================================================

Jamber Bole
Biographical information
Pseudonyms
Crump
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Family
Bole brothers
Social information
Affiliation
Mott Irregulars
Malaz 14th Army
Occupation(s)
Sapper
Title(s)
High Marshal
"
It weren't my fault.  I ain't never used cussers afore!
"
―Crump
Jamber Bole
, known more commonly as "
Crump
" to the
Malazans
, was a
sapper
in
Sergeant
Cord
's 7th Squad, 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
14th Army
.
He was described as having a long horsey face with strangely wide-spaced eyes, a long, scrawny neck, big ears, and a fist-sized Adam's apple.
He was tall
and had absurdly long legs with wild, knobby knees that came up to his ears when he ran.
He had a broad, mindless smile with huge and gleaming teeth.
He wore huge boots.
Crump was originally a
High Marshal
in the
Mott Irregulars
from
Mott Wood
.
By his own admission, he had been arrested and been put in manacles by the Irregulars. He removed his restraints with the help of a fish spine and left when no-one was looking.
He was generally considered to be a halfwit, but did possess some skills.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. The
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
was to begin with the Malazan sappers each placing a timed
wall-breaker munition
at the base of the city's wall.
Ebron
forewarned
Bottle
, who was to disguise the sappers' approach with his magic, to beware of Crump, saying he was dangerous. At the wall, Crump revealed he had amassed more than his share of munitions, placing three wall-breakers and setting their fuses off early.
Cuttle
called for an immediate and hasty retreat, but many soldiers caught up in the ensuing massive explosion died.
Crump survived and returned to his squad.
First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the
Heavy infantry
.
Fist
Keneb
then ordered Cord to lead the 9th Company's seventh through twelfth
medium infantry
squads into Y'Ghatan.
Once inside the city, the Malazans immediately came under heavy attack by hidden swordsmen and archers. Cord's squad linked up with
Mosel
's heavy infantry following
Fiddler
's marines.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap. The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. Cord's squad fled the flames along with a mixed group of survivors from
Sobelone
's,
Balm
's, Fiddler's,
Hellian
's, and
Gesler
's squads. The intense flames drove the soldiers to the Temple of the
Queen of Dreams
where Gesler thought to somehow make a bargain with the goddess.  Their hopes were dashed when Crump urinated on the altar causing it to crack. Cuttle chose the moment to have words over the explosion at the wall, but Crump insisted it was not his fault because he had never used cussers before.
Crump was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city. They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
. During the ordeal, Crump crawled behind Gesler annoying him with his idiotic songs.
When the group found and ingested an ancient cache of
Carelbarra
,
Stump Flit
appeared to Crump in a drug-induced dream. The Salamander God revealed that he was being pursued by his fellow
Bole brothers
and that his future would take a rather bleak turn if they caught up with him.
Unaware that any had survived, the 14th Army made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
.
Faradan Sort
and
Sinn
remained behind and discovered the survivors as they crawled from the wreckage.
Crump and the others made the long march west, finally catching up to the army on the coast.
After the encounter between Nok's Imperial Fleet and the
Third Edur Imperial Fleet
in the Kokakal Sea, Crump waved at the enemy
Tiste Edur
earning a fist to the head from Cord. As the sergeant cursed him out, Crump listened with a broad, mindless smile and an expression that twitched in "sheer delight every time Cord's tirade reached new heights of imagination."
Nok's fleet returned to
Malaz City
where the Adjunct met with Empress
Laseen
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress Laseen at Malaz City and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the Tiste Edur fleet that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
to invade the
Letherii Empire
.
Cord and Balm's squads took the
Silanda
to the island of
Second Maiden Fort
off the coast of Lether to establish a headquarters and resupply base for the Adjunct.
They found the island on the verge of being destroyed under a mountain of ice released by the collapse of
Gothos
' ancient
Omtose Phellack
ritual, but Sinn was able to hold the ice back with her magic until its force was spent. The island's self-declared ruler,
Brullyg
, gratefully welcomed the Malazans as royal guests until they placed him under house arrest and secretly took control of the island.
Crump, Shard and Sinn by
Shadaan
While Balm's squad kept Brullyg under guard and monitored the island from its only town, Cord's squad patrolled the island's coast and interior while awaiting Tavore's arrival.
Cord kept Crump busy digging deep holes to keep him out of trouble and with the hopes that one would eventually collapse and bury him alive. The sapper sung endless mad swamp songs while he worked irritating the rest of the squad. When Crump excitedly found a hoard of infant skulls that stirred to life, Cord hurriedly ordered him to fill all the holes in.
Meanwhile Tavore sent Fist Keneb's marines to the mainland, spreading them in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast and burning their
transport vessels
behind them. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Shurq Elalle
and her ship,
Undying Gratitude
, were caught up in the Malazan blockade of Second Maiden Fort's port. When Adjunct Tavore arrived with the rest of the Malazan fleet, she hired the pirate to guide them to the mouth of the
Lether River
leading to Letheras.
Cord and Balm's squads made the journey on the
Silanda
and Masan Gilani kept Cord company as he manned the ship's steering oar. She was trying to avoid the unwanted interest of Balm's squad and especially Crump, who had decided she was worthy of worship, claiming she had "the tail of some salamander god." When Gilani rejected Cord's own romantic advances, he suggested she take another look at Crump. Gilani was initially disgusted by the idea until Cord piqued her interest by saying "Crump's no whiskered shrew under those breeches." When she departed he excitedly began plotting a betting pool for how long it would be before she ran away screaming from the sapper.
Meanwhile, Ebron and the other squad members killed time on deck trying to cheat Crump in games of
Bones
. The mage complained that the sapper's luck was uncanny, defying even his attempts to sway the bones and scull with magic. He concluded Crump might really be a member of the legendary mage-hunting
Bole brothers
as he claimed. Ebron told Cord that Crump had already won more than three hundred
imperial jakatas
in the game that was rigged against him.
The Adjunct's fleet made landfall near Letheras and defeated the city's
Imperial Brigade
. During the fighting, Crump was seen rushing up the slope at the enemy carrying a cusser in each hand. The resulting avalanche of Letherii body parts buried him until the sapper could climb his way out with a great big grin on his face.
Meanwhile, Keneb's marines secretly entered the city to secure its western gate to allow the rest of the army entrance.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
(Information needed)
In
The Crippled God
(Information needed)
Crump's song excerpts
Excerpt 1
"
and I says oh I says them marsh trees
got soft feet, and moss beards all the way down
and they sway in the smelly breeze
from that swamp water all yella'n'brown
oh we was in the froggy toady dawn
belly-down in the leeches and collectin' spawn
'cause when you give those worms a squeeze
the blue pinky ropes come slimin' down—
and don't they taste sweet!
and don't they taste sweet!
sweet as peat, oh yes
sweet as peat—'
and I says oh I says that ole bridge
got feeta stone, and mortar white as bone
and the badgers dangle from the ledge
swingin' alla day alla way home
oh we was pullin' vines from you know where
and stuffin' our ears with sweety sweet loam
jus t'get them badgers flyin' outa there
inta them cook pots in the hearthy home—
and don't they taste sweet!
and don't they taste sweet!
sweet as peat, oh yes
sweet as peat—
and I says oh I says that warlock's tower—
"
―Crump
Excerpt 2
"
Shillydan the dark-eyed man
Pokes his head up for a look round
Hillyman the black-clawed man
Came up the well for a look around
"Well and and!" says the twelve-toed man
And round down the hill he bound
Still-me-hand the dead-smile man
Went bounding bound down he did bound
Shillydan the red-water man
Croaks and kisses the lass's brow
Hillyman the blue-cocked man
Strokes and blessings t'thank 'er now!
"
―Crump
Trivia
In response to a fan question,
Steven Erikson
stated that Crump likely saved Malazan lives at Y'Ghatan with his overzealous bombing of the walls. The resulting crater slowed the Malazan advance into the city preventing more from being caught up by the fires.
