Lutes
was the squad healer for
Borduke
's 6th squad
marines
of the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
.
He was described as "a quiet, small man".
In
House of Chains
Lutes was part of
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
's punitive expedition against the
Army of the Apocalypse
.  On the road from
Aren
to
Raraku
, he and
Balgrid
helped Borduke inspect the entrants chosen for the 9th Company
Scorpion
fights.
He was likely either the Holder or Trainer for the 6th squad's entrant,
Mangonel
.
When
Leoman
and his two hundred desert warriors launched a surprise pre-dawn attack on the Malazan camp, Borduke's squad grabbed their
Crossbows
and prepared to fire on the warriors as they rode past their tents.
Maybe
fired early, spoiling his squad's attack and allowing
Corabb
to make a spectacular escape.  Lutes threw his crossbow to the ground in disgust, earning a rebuke from Borduke.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
, Leoman led the Army of the Apocalypse westward towards
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. On the march, Lutes and Maybe found a huge scorpion of a type unknown to them to replace Mangonel.  But before they could place
Sparkle
into the ring,
Bottle
informed them to spread the word that the competition was off.  New company
Captain
Faradan Sort
had deliberately crushed Joyful Union under her heel. Bottle advised them to get rid of the female scorpion before its distress scent attracted hundreds or thousands of aggressive males.
In the hours before
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
, Lutes was unable to eat and felt sick. Maybe's talk of the dangers and bloody effects of misfired
Moranth Mountains
sent Lutes vomiting and the other members of Borduke's squad experienced "sympathetic heaves".  Borduke stormed off in disgust.
Adjunct Tavore launched the attack on Y'Ghatan by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, with Borduke's squad first into the breach.  But just as they cleared the wall's rubble, they were ambushed by archers and swordsmen.  Borduke,
Ibb
, and
Hubb
were killed immediately.
Fiddler
launched a
cusser
from his
Crossbow
into the windows of the building above them that accidentally killed several members of
Mosel
's squad and left
Balgrid
deafened. Lutes was injured as well, although it was unclear whether from the ambush or Fiddler's attack.
Lutes was pulled clear, then left to be retrieved by a following squad.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap.  The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno.  A small group of soldiers survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city.  They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
.
Unaware that any had survived, the 14th Army made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
.
Faradan Sort
and
Sinn
remained behind and discovered the survivors as they crawled from the wreckage.
Captain
Sort reorganised the shattered soldiers, placing Lutes into
Hellian
's squad.
On the long trek across the desert, Lutes and
Deadsmell
did their best to tend to the survivors.
In
Reaper's Gale
Lutes was reassigned to Hellian's 8th squad.
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
On the night of the marines' landing on the coast, a drunken Hellian ordered her squad to each pack one of her casks of ale. Lutes noted that she was poisoning her liver and they briefly argued over whether the organ could be physically squeezed out to effect sobriety.
Urb
's 13th squad found them there and both squads remained together for the march inland.
At
Boaral Keep
they ambushed a troop of unsuspecting Edur with Lutes delivering a spectacular crossbow shot to the chest of
Preda
Estav Kendar
. Hellian told
Tavos Pond
that Lutes had balanced his weapon on her back as she vomited to make the shot. At Hellian's suggestion they acquired the Edur's mounts and pushed hard inland for the capital, fighting from tavern to tavern.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
As the marines neared
Letheras
fighting became more desperate, although Hellian earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler and
Gesler
's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
Lutes was cut to pieces alongside Tavos Pond as the two soldiers tried to hold a flank in the mouth of an alleyway.

======================================================================
PAGE: Madan'Tul Rada
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Madan'Tul_Rada
======================================================================

Madan'Tul Rada
[MAD-un TOOL RAD-uh]
(sometimes spelled
Madan'tul Rada
or
Madan tul'Rada
) was a
Lieutenant
of the
Malazan
14th Army
. He was newly under the command of
Captain
Faradan Sort
at the time of the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
in
Seven Cities
. Although she found his name a mouthful, Captain Sort (usually) appreciated his taciturn nature.
He carried a round shield.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. During the worst of the firestorm at the Siege of Y'Ghatan, it looked like Madan'Tul Rada and the rest of the soldiers under Faradan Sort's command were going to be fatally overcome by fire. But first the lieutenant, and then the captain, saw the young mage
Sinn
"dancing, yet not burning" in the flames. The sight was so amazing, that Madan'Tul was prompted to ask, "How did she do that?"
Sort quickly directed Sinn to create a tunnel through the flames so that the Malazans could make their escape.
Once the battle was over,
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
and the rest of her officers prepared to move the army on, convinced that none of the missing could possibly have survived the holocaust. Faradan Sort remained behind without authorization, following Sinn to the still smoldering ruin of Y'Ghatan to see if they could find any survivors among the soldiers feared lost.
Madan'Tul Rada was subsequently promoted to captain,
presumably triggered by Sort's seeming desertion.
Lieutenant
Pores
later saw the new captain engaged in conversation with
Ruthan Gudd
,
Kindly
,
Gall
, and
Imrahl
on the shore of the
Kokakal Sea
as they waited for
Admiral
Nok
's fleet.
In
Reaper's Gale
Madan'Tul Rada was again Faradan Sort's lieutenant (after his brief promotion to captain in Seven Cities).
During the Bonehunter invasion of
Letherii Empire
, it was
Throatslitter
's opinion that the lieutenant was one of several officers who should be promoted to the rank of
Fist
by Adjunct Tavore in place of Fists like
Blistig
, who had lost their hope and spirit.
In
Dust of Dreams
Madan's arrival at an overpriced, upscale tavern in
Letheras
was noticed by Fist
Keneb
, who pointed him out to Fist Blistig. Since this particular drinking establishment was not of the sort to attract the custom of any Malazan soldiers below the rank of captain, it had become the 'officer's tavern', attracting the Fists, especially, of the
Bonehunters
--thus Madan would almost certainly have to have been of the rank of captain, or above.
Trivia
Madan'Tul Rada receives three different spellings of his name across the three novels in which he appears. In all of his appearances in the text of
The Bonehunters
the letter "T" is capitalised in his name (i.e., Madan'Tul Rada). In
Reapers's Gale
, he appears in the Dramatis Personae with a lower case "t" (i.e., Madan'tul Rada) and in his single appearance in the text as the even more different "Madan tul'Rada". In
Dust of Dreams
, he is simply referred to as Madan.

PAGE: Masan Gilani
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Masan_Gilani

Masan Gilani
Biographical information
Race
Human
(
Dal Honese
)
Gender
Female
Social information
Affiliation
Malaz 14th Army
Occupation(s)
Soldier
Masan Gilani
was a
Dal Honese
Heavy infantry
soldier in the
Malaz 14th Army
. She likely belonged to either
Sergeant
Sobelone
's or Sergeant
Tugg
's squad.
She was described as tall and dark-skinned with heavy, shapely breasts, a swell to her belly and hips, and graceful long legs with leonine lines.
She also had elongated, almond-shaped eyes
and was generally considered very beautiful.
Her voice was said to be luscious and heavenly.
She was also a skilled rider.
A large hooked-blade was part of her gear.
She carried two vicious-looking
long-knives
in scabbards on her hips.
History
As a young woman, she had left her two children in the care of her aunts and uncles and departed the
Dal Hon Plains
.  After Dal Hon had been conquered by the
Malazan Empire
it was increasingly common for Dal Honese to take the path of wandering, a custom by which Masan Gilani chose to explore the world and join the army.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. Adjunct Tavore launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the heavy and
medium infantry
. Once inside the city, the Malazans immediately came under heavy attack by hidden swordsmen and archers. Both Sergeants Sobelone and Tugg were killed.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap. The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. Masan Gilani fled the flames along with a mixed group of survivors from Sobelone's, Tugg's,
Fiddler
's,
Hellian
's, and
Gesler
's squads. She was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city. They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
.
Unaware that any had survived, the 14th Army made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
.
Faradan Sort
and
Sinn
remained behind and discovered the survivors as they crawled from the wreckage.
Captain
Sort reorganised the shattered soldiers, promoting
Urb
to sergeant and placing Gilani in his newly created 13th squad.
Masan Gilani by
Jason Dement
The survivors followed the 14th Army's trail west. During that journey their officers selected Masan Gilani, as the best rider, to take
Apsalar
's horse and her
Kethra knife
and ride ahead to try and catch up to and notify the army of their survival.
Along the way she was stopped short when her mount was attacked and killed by the starving and feverish
Dejim Nebrahl
. She was able to slay one of the
T'rolbarahl
's
D'ivers
forms and cripple another, but only managed to escape when the
Hounds of Shadow
and the
Deragoth
intervened. Both sets of Hounds had been on their own hunts for the T'rolbarahl.
The wounded Gilani was forced to wait for the others to catch up to her on foot, so that
Deadsmell
could tend to her. Apsalar allowed her to keep the kethra knife.
Then they resumed their journey to rejoin the 14th Army on the coast.
Aboard one of Nok's ships, Sinn snuggled under Gilani's cloak to fondle and suckle her breasts. Neither Gilani nor Sinn's brother,
Shard
, felt moved to stop her.
Gilani also spent her time aboard ship sewing badges bearing the
Bonehunters
' new official sigil.
Nok's fleet returned the army to
Malaz City
where the Adjunct met with Empress
Laseen
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress Laseen at Malaz City and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
to invade the
Letherii Empire
.
Masan Gilani was originally a heavy, but after the reorganisation of the army for the invasion of Lether, she became a
marine
and was temporarily reassigned to
Balm
's squad.
Rumour among the soldiers was that she had shifted to Balm's squad because she found Urb so handsome she could not think straight around him.
Balm and
Cord
's squads took the
Silanda
to the island of
Second Maiden Fort
off the coast of Lether to establish a headquarters and resupply base for the Adjunct.
They found the island on the verge of being destroyed under a mountain of ice released by the collapse of
Gothos
' ancient
Omtose Phellack
ritual, but
Sinn
was able to hold the ice back with her magic until its force was spent. The island's self-declared ruler,
Brullyg
, gratefully welcomed the Malazans as royal guests until they placed him under house arrest and secretly took control of the island.
Balm's squad kept Brullyg under guard and monitored the island from its only town, as Cord's squad patrolled the island's coast and interior while awaiting Tavore's arrival.
Sinn served as a go-between, able to transport herself instantly across the island with her magic.
Masan Gilani spent most of her time in town, but she and
Widdershins
sometimes accompanied Cord's squad as needed.
She,
Galt
, and
Lobe
all served as muscle in Brullyg's chambers, but the voluptuous Gilani's charms also kept Brullyg stupid and docile.
Among Cord's squad, she was likely the only one not to fear Sinn and her growing power.
She still thought of the budding
High Mage
as the little mute child who had suckled in her arms.
Meanwhile Tavore sent Fist Keneb's marines to the mainland, spreading them in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast and burning their
transport vessels
behind them. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
When Adjunct Tavore arrived with the rest of the Malazan fleet, she hired
Shurq Elalle
to guide them to the mouth of the
Lether River
leading to Letheras.
Balm and Cord's squads made the journey on the
Silanda
. Masan Gilani refused to wear her armour on board for fear of drowning and spent time with Cord on deck to avoid attention from the men of her squad as well as
Crump
, the sapper. Cord pointed out Captain
Kindly
drooling over her from the nearby
Froth Wolf
before making an advance of his own towards her. When Gilani expressed no romantic interest in Cord, he intrigued her by suggesting she take up with Crump. Gilani was initially disgusted by the idea until Cord piqued her interest by saying "Crump's no whiskered shrew under those breeches." Then he excitedly began plotting a betting pool for how long it would be before she ran away screaming from the sapper. Meanwhile, Kindly ordered
Lieutenant
Pores
to prepare a disciplinary report on Gilani for being out of uniform.
The Adjunct's fleet made landfall near Letheras in time to see a massive release of enemy sorcery near Fist Keneb's reported position. Believing the marines had been wiped out, Tavore's forces defeated the city's
Imperial Brigade
.
Balm's squad, along with Masan Gilani, secured horses to chase down fleeing Letherii soldiers. They continued further inland towards the city with Gilani in the lead and Balm mesmerized by her bottom. When they arrived at the field where
Beak
had saved Keneb's marines, they were mystified to find no bodies.
Approaching the city's western gate, they found it in control of Keneb's troops. By this time, "the Confusion" had come upon Balm and he tackled Gilani from her horse to save her from nonexistent enemies. Deadsmell assured Keneb the sergeant would snap out of it soon, as the Fist ordered Masan Gilani to race back to fetch reinforcements from Tavore.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
Masan Gilani was persuaded by
Sinter
, who had had a premonition, to leave the Bonehunters in search of allies. She found the
T'lan Imass
of the
Unbound
.
In
The Crippled God
Masan Gilani by
Dejan Delic
On the return journey to the Bonehunters, Masan Gilani and the Unbound came across the site of the army's battle with the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
. Seeing the battlefield seething with orthens, she told the Unbound that she would not eat orthen anymore and questioned that crossing a lizard with a rat had been a good idea in the first place.

======================================================================
PAGE: Masker
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Masker
======================================================================

Masker
was a
Heavy
in
Sergeant
Primly
's 10th squad in the
8th Legion
, 3rd Company of the
Bonehunters
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the
marines
in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Primly's 10th squad, along with
Sinter
's 4th and
Badan Gruk
's 5th squads, landed furthest south of all the marines. Remaining together, they saw little resistance moving east and soon reached a river. Rather than slog through through waist-deep swamp muck, they stole a fisher boat and sailed upriver. They made excellent time until running into a Letherii galley in the night. Sinter and
Kisswhere
were lost in the water during a discharge of
Moranth munitions
. Forced ashore, they were pursued day and night, using up their mages dodging and ducking enemy attacks. Masker perished either during the river battle or the pursuit that followed.
When
Lookback
later began grumbling about pursuing a deadly vendetta against
Gesler
and
Stormy
,
Drawfirst
theorised he would not be talking that way if Masker's death had not left him as the last heavy in Primly's squad.

======================================================================
PAGE: Maybe
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Maybe
======================================================================

Maybe
was a
Marine
Sapper
in the 6th squad, 9th Company of the
8th Legion
in the
Malaz 14th Army
.
He was originally from
Aren
,
and was well known for his ability to retain facts.
Maybe had pale green eyes and became physically sickened in the presence of magic.
Before the 14th Army's uniform was standardised, he wore a brass loop on one ear from which hung a human finger bone.
In
House of Chains
Maybe was part of
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
's punitive expedition against the
Army of the Apocalypse
. He was placed in
Borduke
's squad.
While the 14th Army was still in
Aren
, Maybe stood guard duty with
Balgrid
outside the 9th Company's improvised barracks. Balgrid was magically disguised as a bale of hay when their post was approached by
Pearl
and
Lostara Yil
. Maybe was impressed that Balgrid's disguise had fooled a real live
Claw
, but Pearl later confided to a confused Lostara that he had noticed two guards at the gate.
At
Vathar Crossing
,
Fiddler
and
Cuttle
used
Moranth munitions
to clear the debris blocking the river's ford.  Maybe critiqued their work before rolling his eyes at their advice on crossing the river. Fiddler muttered that he hated "satirical bastards like him".
When
Leoman
and his two hundred desert warriors launched a surprise pre-dawn attack on the Malazan camp, Borduke's squad grabbed their
Crossbows
and prepared to fire on the warriors as they rode past their tents. Maybe fired early, foiling his squad's attack and allowing
Corabb
to make a spectacular escape.
Maybe was chosen as the bet-holder for the 9th Company
Scorpion
fights because of his superior memory. He silently repeated numbers and names to himself during the competition.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
, Leoman led the Army of the Apocalypse westward towards
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. On the march, Maybe and Lutes found a huge scorpion of a type unknown to them to replace Mangonel. But before they could place
Sparkle
into the ring,
Bottle
informed them to spread the word that the competition was off. New company
Captain
Faradan Sort
had deliberately crushed Joyful Union under her heel. Bottle advised them to get rid of the female scorpion before its distress scent attracted hundreds or thousands of aggressive males.
In the hours before
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
, Maybe and Lutes were unable to eat and felt sick. Maybe's talk of the dangers and bloody effects of misfired
Moranth Mountains
sent Lutes vomiting and the other members of Borduke's squad experienced "sympathetic heaves". Borduke stormed off in disgust.
Adjunct Tavore launched the attack on Y'Ghatan by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, with Borduke's squad first into the breach.  But just as they cleared the wall's rubble, they were ambushed by archers and swordsmen. Borduke,
Ibb
, and
Hubb
were killed immediately while Lutes was injured and had to be pulled from the fighting.  Maybe and the other able survivors then tagged along with Fiddler's squad.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap. The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. Maybe fled the flames along with a mixed group of survivors from Fiddler's,
Gesler
's,
Cord
's, and
Hellian
's squads. He was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city. They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
.
Unaware that any had survived, the 14th Army made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
.
Faradan Sort
and
Sinn
remained behind and discovered the survivors as they crawled from the wreckage.
Captain
Sort reorganised the shattered soldiers, placing Maybe into Hellian's squad.
Touchy
and
Brethless
squabbled over who would replace the promoted
Urb
as Hellian's
corporal
, so Hellian promoted them both. Maybe spoke for the other soldiers newly assigned to Hellian's squad when he accepted the dual promotion saying, "idiots make good corporals" and "we ain't gonna listen to you anyways."
Nok's fleet returned the army to
Malaz City
where the Adjunct met with Empress
Laseen
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress Laseen at Malaz City and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Fist
Keneb
followed in their wake with six squads of marines, while Captain
Faradan Sort
and
Beak
attempted to keep lines of communication open between both groups.
Maybe joined Sergeant
Hellian
's 8th squad, though she always had trouble remembering his name because she thought it "stupid".
Hellian's squad was paired with Urb's for the landings. When they assembled on the beach, Urb found her arranging casks of rum she had salvaged from the burning ships amongst her squad.
The two squads remained together and Balgrid and
Bowl
used magic to cover their tracks.
After the squads defeated a troop of Edur at
Boaral Keep
, Maybe searched their pockets for coin but was surprised to find only polished stones. The squads acquired mounts at Hellian's suggestion and pushed hard inland for the capital, fighting from tavern to tavern.
The two squads began taking trophies of ears and fingers and tying them to their belts, although Maybe had to give up on an Edur head that pulled his breaches down.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
As the marines neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and they began taking casualties. Hellian earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, moneylenders, and debt-holders in each village. Then her squad stayed in the village tavern--decorated with the severed heads of their victims--until it was dry before moving on to the next.
Fiddler and
Gesler
's squads found them drinking and singing at a tavern a day's travel from the capital. Fiddler did not approve, but could not argue with Hellian's success where all the other squads had failed miserably.
Almost as soon as the marines were reunited, a force of hundreds of Edur enveloped the village.
The Edur were repelled by the arrival of
Badan Gruk
,
Sinter
, and
Primly
's fresh squads.
The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by Fist Keneb.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under Beak's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white.
The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Hellian, Urb, Fiddler, and Gesler's squads were sent into the city to cause trouble while the remaining marines opened the city's west gate to Tavore's infantry. Hellian's squad quickly disappeared into a local tavern where she threatened to hang a
Letherii barkeep
unless he revealed the tavern's hidden stock.
After the main force of Malazans entered the city, the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
(Information needed)
In
The Crippled God
(Information needed)
Quotes
Pearl
: "
And have you a name, soldier?
"
Maybe
: "
Maybe.
"
Pearl
: "
Well, what is it?
"
Maybe
: "
I just told you. Maybe. Do you need me to spell it out or something?
"
Pearl
: "
Can you?
"
―Pearl meets Maybe

======================================================================
PAGE: Mayfly
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Mayfly
======================================================================

"
So who needs brains to soldier? They just get in the way of soldierin' and it's no good things gettin' in the way...If soldiers thought too much about what they're doin', they wouldn't fight no more.
"
―Mayfly
Mayfly
was a
Heavy
in the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
. She was part of
Sergeant
Mosel
's squad.
She was described as easily confused, but as tough as they came.
She had broken her nose more times than she could count and found the clicking noises associated with readjusting it to be vaugely satisfying.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. Once the 14th Army reached the city's outskirts, Mosel and his squad decided to take revenge on the wagon whose dust they had eaten over many long miles. They bound and gagged the wagoner and the load crew in the long grass before proceeding to pry the wagon apart. Under Mosel's watchful eye, Mayfly and
Flashwit
pried the nails, studs, and fittings from the wagon's boards while
Taffo
and
Uru Hela
struggled with an axle.
While they worked, they discussed Nefarias Bredd sightings with
Bottle
. Flashwit thought Mayfly had seen him, but Mayfly said she had half heard it from
Smiles
. Mayfly hoped to one day "roll in the blankets" with Bredd.
Adjunct Tavore launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the heavy and
medium infantry
. Once inside the city, the Malazans immediately came under attack from swordsmen on the ground and archers in the buildings above them. Mosel's squad of heavies waded into the swordsmen just as
Fiddler
launched a
cusser
from his
Crossbow
into the windows of the building above them. The resulting explosion killed
Harbyn
and Taffo, leaving only Mayfly, Flashwit, and Uru Hela. An angry Mosel descended on Fiddler before the continued fighting pulled him and his squad away.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap.  The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. At some point, Mosel was killed
and his three heavies joined a mixed group of survivors from
Cord
's, Fiddler's, and
Borduke
's squads. They fled the flames while Mayfly, Flashwit, Uru Hela , and
Shortnose
— armed only with knives and fists — defended the group against a score of fanatics. Mayfly took a blow to her neck from a spear shaft that struck Uru Hela.
Mayfly was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city. They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
.
Unlike most of the other survivors, she had not found the fires or the tunnels much to fear.
Unaware that any had survived, the 14th Army made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
.
Faradan Sort
and
Sinn
remained behind and discovered the survivors as they crawled from the wreckage.
Captain
Sort reorganised the shattered soldiers, placing Mayfly into
Gesler
's Fifth squad.
After the survivors rejoined the 14th Army on the coast of the
Kokakal Sea
, Gesler and
Stormy
were given back command of the
Silanda
. Mayfly served aboard the vessel along with
Balm
and Fiddler's squads on the return voyage to
Quon Tali
.
Some festering argument between Shortnose and Flashwit led to a brawl on the deck that expanded to include Balm's squad as well. In the melee, Mayfly threw
Lobe
in the air onto the pile of animated heads on the
Silanda's
deck.
The Adunct's fleet travelled to
Malaz City
where Empress
Laseen
awaited Tavore in
Mock's Hold
. The
Silanda
joined Tavore's flagship, the
Froth Wolf
, to moor at the city pier while the rest of the fleet remained anchored in the harbour.  The entire city seethed with magically induced anger against the 14th Army and the soldiers of the
Silanda
prepared to defend their ship from the mob after the Adjunct was escorted away.  Mayfly, Shortnose, Uru Hela,
Tarr
,
Corabb Bhilan Thenu'alas
, and Flashwit formed a shield wall that took the brunt of the mob's attack.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress Laseen at Malaz City and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
By this time, Mayfly was reassigned to Gesler and Stormy's squad.
Stormy happily came to think of his three female heavies as the "dread ladies", who could "stare down a rutting
bhederin
bull and beat it into a pulp".
Gesler and Fiddler's squads remained together and at first had no problem remaining hidden from enemy soldiers.
But the Letherii soon became aware of the enemy operating in their territory. Only
Corabb
's impossible luck saved them from a clever ambush in the forest when he accidentally flushed out a deer that immediately fell with twenty arrows in it. Mayfly joined Stormy and the other heavies in breaking one side of the ambush, while the other Malazans fired crossbows and sharpers at the enemy. The Malazans quickly turned the attack until the Letherii unveiled their sorcery of grey chaotic fire, killing
Sands
. Fiddler fired a cusser into the trees above the Letherii mage killing him and shredding a score of enemy soldiers before the Malazans were forced to retreat.
Gesler and Fiddler stopped their squads at an isolated farmhouse to lay a trap for a troop of mounted pursuers. While Fiddler and
Cuttle
assembled
The Drum
out of
munitions
, Gesler sent Uru Hela to investigate the occupants of the nearby farmhouse. When the heavy was only fifteen paces from the front door, an enormous
Kenryll'ah demon prince
burst out of the house to kill her with a two-handed wood-axe. Mayfly and the other heavies flanked Stormy as they charged the demon, chopping it with their swords before Gesler called the retreat.
Ironically, the demon and its fellow prince had taken up residence in the farmhouse to retire in peace. They had just wanted to be left alone and the encounter was a tragic accident.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
As the marines neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and Gesler and Fiddler's squads became separated.
Mayfly's armour was destroyed in the fighting and her back was a shredded mess.
A day's travel from the capital, Gesler's squad stumbled upon a village occupied by
Hellian
's squad and a number of others. Gesler and Fiddler's squad reunited at the local tavern just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village. Mayfly was stabbed four times while defending the tavern alongside Stormy, who was surprised she could still stand. Yet she still found time to return her corporal's sword that had been lost in the melee.
The Edur were repelled by the arrival of
Badan Gruk
,
Sinter
, and
Primly
's fresh squads.
The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by Fist Keneb.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Gesler, Fiddler,
Urb
, and Hellian's squads were sent into the city to cause trouble while the remaining marines opened the city's west gate to Tavore's infantry. Gesler's squad soon became separated from Fiddler's after the two squads teamed to ambush an assembly of the city's Main Garrison.
After the main force of Malazans entered the city, the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
(Information needed)
In
The Crippled God
Mayfly and
Flashwit
survived the battle with the
K'Chain Nah'ruk.
They joined
Gaunt-Eye
's 18th squad together with survivors of other squads, like
Skulldeath
and
Drawfirst
, to make up numbers.
The 18th Squad joined the rest of the heavies and marines in the final defence of
Kaminsod's
heart.

======================================================================
PAGE: Mosel
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Mosel
======================================================================

Sergeant
Mosel
was a
heavy
infantryman of the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
.
He was a typical mixed breed from
Malaz City
. Mosel was described as lean, with epicanthic folds in his eyes that spoke of
Kanese
blood. He wore his hair braided and cut finger-length in the fashion of
Jakatakan
pirates.
He was younger than his fellow sergeant,
Sobelone
. Sergeant
Tugg
was bigger than both of them.
The three had a threatening air about them that had less to do with size than attitude, and were similar enough in look that they could almost be siblings.
Mosel was protective of the soldiers under his command, always vigilant for any notion that someone was mocking them.
Known members of Mosel's squad
Corporal
Harbyn
Flashwit
Mayfly
Taffo
Uru Hela
In
House of Chains
Mosel's squad was part of
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
's punitive expedition against the
Army of the Apocalypse
.  There had been a restructuring of the 8th Legion and soon after the army arrived at
Raraku
, several of the sergeants from those squads who would join the
Marines
of 9th Company dropped in on
Strings
to introduce themselves. Amongst them were Mosel and his fellow sergeants, Sobelone and Tugg.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the Army of the Apocalypse westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed.  Once the 14th Army reached the city's outskirts, Mosel and his squad decided to take revenge on the wagon whose dust they had eaten over many long miles. They bound and gagged the wagoner and the load crew in the long grass before proceeding to pry the wagon apart. Under Mosel's watchful eye,
Flashwit
and
Mayfly
pried the nails, studs, and fittings from the wagon's boards while
Taffo
and
Uru Hela
struggled with an axle.
While they worked, they discussed
Nefarias Bredd
sightings with
Bottle
.
Adjunct Tavore launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan marines, followed quickly by the heavy and
medium infantry
. Once inside the city, the Malazans immediately came under attack from swordsmen on the ground and archers in the buildings above them.  Mosel's squad of heavies waded into the swordsmen just as
Fiddler
launched a
cusser
from his
Crossbow
into the windows of the building above them.  The resulting explosion killed
Harbyn
and Taffo. An angry Mosel descended on Fiddler before the continued fighting pulled him away.
In later fighting, Flashwit, Mayfly, and Uru Hela were depicted as fighting alongside Fiddler's squad, but Mosel was not mentioned.  Fiddler later confirmed that Mosel was killed during the battle.

======================================================================
PAGE: Mud
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Mud
======================================================================

Mud
was a member of
Sergeant
Moak
's
Medium infantry
squad of the 9th Company,
8th Legion
in the
Malaz 14th Army
.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. Upon reaching the outskirts of the city, Moak prepared a stew for his squad using a ripened fish he had carried for weeks.  When his squad all "got the squats", he blamed it on their weak stomachs while a true soldier like himself suffered only from belches that smelled of rotting fish guts.
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the
heavy
and medium infantry. Barely a street in and fearing an ambush, Sergeant
Gesler
called up Moak's squad as well as
Thom Tissy
's sappers and
Tugg
's heavies to clear the surrounding buildings. In the fighting that followed, the poorly trained sappers misfired their
munitions
. One shrieking sapper exited the building fully aflame.  As Moak's squad went to help him, the sapper's munitions satchel went off killing Mud and Moak's entire squad.

======================================================================
PAGE: Mudslinger
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Mudslinger
======================================================================

Mudslinger
was a
Malazan
marine
.
Braven Tooth
called him a tough one and a survivor.
In
House of Chains
Mudslinger was stranded on
Drift Avalii
together with
Traveller
,
Hawl
, and other surviving
marines
after their fleet had had a chance encounter with
Tiste Edur
ships.
Cutter
sought out the Malazan survivors to aid
Darist
and the
Tiste Andii
in their defence of the island's
Throne of Shadow
against Edur attack.  The Malazans decided to defend the island at Traveller's insistence.  As Mudslinger had been wounded in the naval battle, he was left behind.  The others were cut down by the Edur.
In
The Bonehunters
It transpired that Mudslinger was one of a half-dozen Malazan survivors of the battle on Drift Avalii.  Afterwards, Traveller had ordered the Malazans to leave the island aboard one of the Tiste Edur dromons while he continued to defend the island on his own.  When they left, their ship was hit by a storm. The survivors were washed ashore on an atoll where they spent months drinking coconut milk and eating clams. Eventually they were rescued and brought to
Malaz City
by the
Jakatakan Fleet
.
Mudslinger and fellow castaway,
Gentur
, became regulars together at
Coop
's
Hanged Man Inn
. Among the clientele, they befriended
Foreigner
and largely tried to avoid
Master Sergeant
Braven Tooth
. Mudslinger had bad memories of training under the Master Sergeant. On the night the
Bonehunters
returned to Malaz City, Braven Tooth recruited the pair to eliminate the
Claw
he spotted tailing his friend
Banaschar
out of the bar.
The pair followed
Saygen Maral
into an alley, but the Claw was aware of them and prepared an ambush.  Gentur died with a tiny quarrel to the base of his skull while Mudslinger ducked to avoid a quarrel to the gut that instead hit above his heart.  Braven Tooth found Mudslinger and found him help before he too perished.
In
Reaper's Gale
Mudslinger joined
Sergeant
Thom Tissy
's 12th Squad of the
8th Legion
, 9th Company of the
Bonehunters
, along with
Corporal
Tulip
,
Ramp
,
Bellig Harn
, Gullstream, and
Bellig Harn
. He served as
Medium infantry
.
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
clashed with Empress
Laseen
at Malaz City and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Fist
Keneb
followed in their wake with six squads of marines, including Tissy's 12th squad.
Once the marines began engaging with the enemy, Keneb had difficulty maintaining contact with his lead elements. Tissy told Keneb that he and the others in the squad understood his anxiety at following impossible orders under difficult conditions. The Fist called him presumptuous and told him to tell his squad to stop theorising.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
As the marines neared Letheras fighting became more desperate, and a large force of Edur stood between Keneb's troops and the forward marines. Thom Tissy heartened the Fist by claiming his troops were ready for a hard fight. They fought their way to a village where all the remaining squads had converged before continuing on together to the capital.
Thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing them towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Thom Tissy's squad was among those sent to secure the city's western gate from the inside to allow the main army entrance into the city. City Garrison soldiers tried to retake the gate in bloody fighting, but Tissy's squad held on long enough for
Balm
's squad, and then others, to arrive.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
Trivia
Although included in the
Dramatis Personae
of
Reaper's Gale
, Mudslinger was not mentioned by name anywhere in the text of the novel.

PAGE: Mulvan Dreader
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters, Humans
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Mulvan_Dreader
======================================================================

Mulvan Dreader
was a squad
mage
with
Primly
's 10th squad,
8th Legion
, 3rd Company in the
Bonehunters
. He specialised in combat magics, but could also perform healing if there was a need.
He was a
Nathii
who had pale skin and black hair.
Beak
identified him as "a Nathii swamp necromancer."
He thought fellow squad mate
Skulldeath
"was truly a man about to explode" for his principled celibacy.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the
marines
in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Primly's squad, along with
Sinter
's 4th and
Badan Gruk
's 5th squads, landed furthest south of all the marines. Remaining together, they saw little resistance moving east and soon reached a river. Rather than slog through through waist-deep swamp muck, they stole a fisher boat and sailed upriver. They made excellent time until running into a Letherii galley in the night.
Kisswhere
and Sinter were lost in the water during a discharge of
Moranth munitions
. Forced ashore, they were pursued day and night, using up their mages dodging and ducking enemy attacks. Somewhere along the way
Masker
was also lost, leaving Primly with only one heavy.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the
Malazan
invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
The marines further north saw intense action, and as they neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and their munition supplies dwindled.
Hellian
and
Urb
's squads earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler
and
Gesler
's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
Three days after leaving the river, Primly, Sinter, and Badan Gruk's squads came upon the overwhelmed Malazans and turned the tide of battle with their fresh supply of munitions. During the fighting, Mulvan Dreader appeared at the badly wounded
Urb
's side, fending off
Hellian
's questions as he saved the sergeant's life. Afterwards, he followed cries for help from a group of soldiers buried beneath a collapsed building. The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by
Fist
Keneb
.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, the seized the city's western gate to allow the rest of the army entrance.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
Mulvan Dreader healed
Pores
after the
lieutenant
was stung by six black wasps. He was ordered to do a testicular inspection of all the squads in his company by
Captain
Kindly
after making a comment under his breath.
In
The Crippled God
He died in the battle against the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Nefarias Bredd
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Nefarias_Bredd
======================================================================

Nefarias Bredd
was a possibly fictitious member of the
Malazan
14th Army's
heavy infantry
. His exploits were legendary, though no one could claim to ever having seen him personally.
In
House of Chains
Sergeant
Moak
mentioned Bredd to his fellow sergeants, asking if anyone had heard of the killer soldier among the heavy infantry, who was supposed to have killed 18 raiders in one night.
Thom Tissy
had also heard the rumour, and elaborated that it had supposedly been 18 one night and 13 the next.
Flashwit
then came in on the conversation and said it had been 50 killed. None of them could make any guess as to which legion, company, or unit Bredd belonged.
In
The Bonehunters
Flashwit told
Uru Hela
and
Smiles
that she had seen Bredd carry one of the Army's dead horses into camp to be roasted for meals.
Sergeant
Mosel
surmised Bredd to be a giant of a man, saying that he must have
Fenn
blood in him. Flashwit heard
Mayfly
had seen him, but Mayfly said she thought it had been
Smiles
who told them about Bredd passing by.  Mayfly hoped to one day "roll in the blankets with that man."
In
Reaper's Gale
Lostara Yil
attributed the joking
Bonehunters
motto 'Last in, looking around' to Nefarias Bredd when pressed on the matter by
Adjunct Tavore
, which elicited a faint smile.
In
Dust of Dreams
After
Master Sergeant
Pores
is blind sided with a sucker punch that leaves him unconscious, his stores wagon is looted. Shortly after he comes to his senses again, he is visited by
Hedge
and four of his new
Bridgeburners
. After eliciting a writ from Pores they inform him about the rumor, that it was Nefarious Bredd who "cracked him one".
In
The Crippled God
A man unknown to
Fiddler
, and claiming to be Nefarias, was seen in the defensive line protecting the
Crippled God
, but he was not seen again. He was described as shorter than
Reliko
, yet pale and thin with a narrow face and protruding ears.
Afterwards,
Tarr
claimed that there was no Nefarias Bredd and that he was made up on the march to
Y'Ghatan
. The soldiers had gotten a bad loaf of bread and someone called it nefarious. It sounded like something
Braven Tooth
would have made up, and they kept the name.
Other rumours
Bredd had no thumbs
and one giant foot, according to Reliko.
A horse had died and Bredd had carried it back to his squad's camp, also according to Flashwit.
Hedge
claimed that he heard through Mayfly that Bredd was "tall but skinny...and his whole face is tiny, like the bud of a flower. With sweet and pleasant eyes and pouty lips."
Quotes
Reliko
: "
...we heard there's a heavy without any thumbs—might be over in Blistig's legion.
"
Fist Keneb
: "
Indeed, and what would his name be
"
Reliko
: "
Nefarias Bredd, sir.
"
Fist Keneb
: "
And how would this soldier be able to wield any weapons, without thumbs?
"
Reliko
: "
Can't say, sir, as I only seen 'im once, and that was from too far away. I expect he ties 'em up sort of, somehow.
"
Fist Keneb
: "
Perhaps, he's missing only one thumb. Shield hand, perhaps.
"
Reliko
: "
Might be, sir, might be, in which case as soon as we find a thumb, why, we'll let him know.
"
―Reliko and Fist Keneb having a typical conversation about Nefarias Bredd
Speculations
For more speculation, visit the following thread on the forum:
Nefarias Bredd... the enigma...
Trivia
Steven Erikson
says "Nefarias Bredd is not a name I can take credit for, as much as I'd like to. It was coined in casual, slightly drunken conversation at a World Fantasy convention, in Montreal, in the hotel bar. I was at the table with fellow author David Keck and a gentleman from England who is now an agent. That gentleman, Darren Nash, made the culinary observation in passing. But I logged it, mused on its deliciousness, then asked Darren for permission to use it. He agreed."
Bredd's first name was sometimes spelled Nefarias and other times Neffarias.
In 2020 a fan asked author Steven Erikson, "Does Nefarias Bredd actually exist or not?" Erikson replied, "[T]he only way I can answer this question is to ask another question...Do any of these characters exist?"
Significant plot details  end here.

Neller
was a
Dal Honese
sapper
in
Primly
's 10th squad,
8th Legion
, 3rd Company of the
Bonehunters
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the
marines
in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Primly's squad, along with
Sinter
's 4th and
Badan Gruk
's 5th squads, landed furthest south of all the marines. Remaining together, they saw little resistance moving east and soon reached a river. Rather than slog through through waist-deep swamp muck, they stole a fisher boat and sailed upriver. They made excellent time until running into a Letherii galley in the night.
Kisswhere
and Sinter were lost in the water during a discharge of
Moranth munitions
. Forced ashore, they were pursued day and night, using up their mages dodging and ducking enemy attacks. Somewhere along the way
Masker
was also lost, leaving Primly with only one heavy.
Neller was friendly with his fellow Dal Hon,
Strap Mull
, from the 4th squad. After Kisswhere's death, the two spoke in their native language about
Corporal
Pravalak Rim
's despair over the woman he had been infatuated with. Neller also wondered if the fighting in Letheras would be anything like
Y'ghatan
, where their squad had done nothing. Strap Mull told him to stop worrying until they got there. Neller carried a sword that Strap Mull had found in a Letherii cabin, but given away once he realised it howled like a wild woman every time it hit something. The sound bothered Strap Mull enough that he stopped his ears with moss whenever he knew Neller planned to use it.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the
Malazan
invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
The marines further north saw intense action, and as they neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and their munition supplies dwindled.
Hellian
and
Urb
's squads earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler
and
Gesler
's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
Three days after leaving the river, Primly, Sinter, and Badan Gruk's squads came upon the overwhelmed Malazans and turned the tide of battle with their fresh supply of munitions. The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by
Fist
Keneb
.

Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, the seized the city's western gate to allow the rest of the army entrance.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
During the battle against the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
, Neller used a
sharper
to blow up one of the lizards, but lost an arm in the explosion. Nah'ruk acidic phlegm had also burnt his eyes and skin.
In
The Crippled God
It was revealed Neller had died, presumably from the wounds suffered in the battle.
Trivia
In
Reaper's Gale
, Neller and Strap Mull refer to Pravalak Rim as "their corporal" despite the fact that only Strap Mull belonged to Pravalak's 4th squad. The
Reaper's Gale
Dramatis Personae lists Neller as part of Primly's 10th squad.

PAGE: Nep Furrow
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters, Humans

Nep Furrow
Biographical information
Race
Human
(
Dal Honese
)
Gender
Male
Social information
Affiliation
Malazan Empire
Bonehunters
Occupation(s)
Mage
Soldier
Nep Furrow
was a
Dal Honese
bush
shaman
and a member of
Badan Gruk
's 5th squad,
8th Legion
, 3rd Company in the
Bonehunters
army. He was described as wrinkled with yellowy eyes, gnarled hands, and pierced everything - ears, nose, wattle, cheeks - the gold ornaments a startling contrast to his dark scowling face.
Bottle
thought his eyes still had the jungle in them.
His accent was so thick as to make many of his utterances completely unintelligible.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the
marines
in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Badan Gruk's squad, along with
Sinter
's 4th and
Primly
's 10th squads, landed furthest south of all the marines. Remaining together, they saw little resistance moving east and soon reached a river. Rather than slog through through waist-deep swamp muck, they stole a fisher boat and sailed upriver. They made excellent time until running into a Letherii galley in the night.
Kisswhere
and Sinter were lost in the water during a discharge of
Moranth munitions
. Forced ashore, they were pursued day and night, using up their mages dodging and ducking enemy attacks. On the first night, Badan Gruk lost his corporal after the man fell down an abandoned well shaft and broke his neck. Badan Gruk chose
Ruffle
to take his place. Somewhere along the way the
Heavy
,
Masker
, was also lost, but Badan Gruk,
Skulldeath
, and others had yet to draw blood.
Skim
teased Nep Furrow asking him to bless her
sharpers
just as he had blessed Kisswhere's before their fatal detonation. She claimed a quick death by munitions was the only way to escape the unwanted advances of
Honey
. The shaman anted nothing to do with her and was clearly made uncomfortable by the "teasin' tit-woman", so she pushed further asking if he had any magicks left in his
blecker
.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the
Malazan
invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
The marines further north saw intense action, and as they neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and their munition supplies dwindled.
Hellian
and
Urb
's squads earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler
and
Gesler
's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
Three days after leaving the river, Badan Gruk, Sinter, and Primly's squads came upon the overwhelmed Malazans and turned the battle with their fresh supply of munitions. The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by
Fist
Keneb
.
Spotting Fiddler, Nep Furrow made a warding gesture and muttered "Yeggetan".
He later complained to Bottle that their predicament could be blamed on Fiddler and the unfinished song he had played in Malaz City. Until it was finished, they would all continue dying.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Badan Gruk's squad was among those sent to secure the city's western gate from the inside to allow the main army entrance into the city. City Garrison soldiers tried to retake the gate in bloody fighting, but Badan Gruk's squad held on long enough for to greet Adjunct Tavore and her group of cavalry when they arrived.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.

Dust of Dreams

In

Nep Furrow Quotes - No definite translations available
Conversation between Nep and
Skim
in
Reaper's Gale
"Eggit'way fra meen, tit-woman!"
(Take it away from me, tit-woman!)
"Wha'?"
(What?)
"You teasin' tit-woman you! Eggit'way fra meen!"
(You teasing tit-woman you! Take it away from me!)
"Bliss'em clay balls? Ya mad, tit-woman? Less time I done that-'"
(Bless those clay balls? Are you mad, tit-woman? Last time I did that-')
"Eggit'way fra meen!"  (Take it away from me, tit-woman!)
Conversation between Nep and
Ruffle
in
The Crippled God

(Why? [...] I am no roach dog, Ruffle. Am a wolf, that's me. Nep Wolf!)
Trivia
Author
Steven Erikson
has said that in at least in one case Nep Furrow's mangled diction was not meant to be translatable into any understandable language and he was having fun with the reader.

======================================================================
PAGE: Nether
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Nether
======================================================================

Nether
Biographical information
Race
Human
(
Wickan
)
Gender
Female
Family
Nil
(twin brother)
Social information
Affiliation
Malazan Empire
Malaz 7th Army
Occupation(s)
Witch
Nether
was a
Wickan
warlock
(or witch)
and twin sister to
Nil
. She had dark skin and eyes "like black liquid". She wore "her hair cut bristly short",
and spoke with a high, piping voice.
Nether was one of the Wickan warlocks reborn and possessed power far stronger than her age would indicate.  She had knowledge empowered by lifetimes.
In
Deadhouse Gates
Nether was around nine or ten years old
when she served in
Sormo E'nath
's cadre of mages. She traveled to
Hissar
on
Seven Cities
to support
Coltaine
, the newly appointed Wickan
Fist
of the
Malaz 7th Army
.  When the
Whirlwind
rebellion drove the Fist out of Hissar, she became one of Coltaine's
Chain of Dogs
.
The Ritual by
Dejan-Delic
After the
Battle of Sekala Crossing
Nether, Nil, and Sormo unleashed the spirits of the land to destroy the
Semk
tribal god.
At the
Battle of Gelor Ridge
she and Nil performed a ritual on the horses of the
Foolish Dog
Clan which allowed them to charge uphill at an unnaturally high speed and strike
Kamist Reloe
's elite infantry legions.
Afterwards, the twins' skin was pale and their hands were stained black and they were confined to bed for days.
Nether accompanied
Duiker
and the Foolish Dog Clan on a mission to secure the crossing over the River
Vathar
. While waiting for Coltaine and the rest of the army to arrive, she admitted to Duiker that the Wickans followed the Fist out of awe. When the Fist bloodied the near-
Ascendant
Gesler
's nose both she and Nil gasped in recognition that Coltaine himself was on the path to Ascendency.
Sormo was killed at the
Battle of Vathar Crossing
, leaving Nether and Nil the army's sole remaining warlocks.
After the
Battle of Sanimon
, Coltaine sent the twins and the refugees ahead of the army along with Duiker and an escort of Wickan youths. Nether and Duiker successfully negotiated with
Kherahn Dhobri
tribe for safe passage and arrived at the gates of
Aren
without major incident.
Nether and Nil stood safely on the walls of Aren as Coltaine and the last of his soldiers were cut down on the plain below. Duiker had to restrain the warlock as she clawed blood from her scalp in grief.
In
House of Chains
Both Nether and Nil were broken by their experience on the Chain of Dogs. Nether allowed her hair to grow into long, greasy ropes, and both twins went about dirty and barefoot.
When
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
arrived in Aren with the
Malaz 14th Army
, neither wanted to accompany the punitive expedition against the
Army of the Whirlwind
. Their magic was no longer strong. They could speak to spirits, but no longer compel them. But as the Adjunct had few mages, she refused to let them return home, holding them to Coltaine's last command and advising them to find a way to awaken the warlock spirits inside themselves.
As the army retraced the Chain of Dogs' steps in reverse, Nether and Nil spent their time attempting to communicate with the spirit of Sormo E'nath.
Fiddler
found the two facing each other over a bronze bowl near the site of
Vathar Crossing
. A swarm of yellow butterflies engulfed the
Bridgeburner
, speaking into his ear. Nether and Nil were heartbroken that the warlock's only contact had been with a stranger, and they demanded to know if Sormo had a message for them. Fiddler concluded that the presence he felt was not Sormo's.
By the time the army arrived at
Raraku
, Nether had grown fuller in appearance, suggesting she was coming of age. Her face took on a permanent expression of severity that left her looking forbidding and burdened. Her hair was shorn close as a vow of grief.
She and her brother confirmed that the Adjunct was right to suspect that the warrior spirits of the desert resisted the
Whirlwind Goddess
' attempt to feed on the land's memories.
On the eve of the
Battle of Raraku
, the boy,
Grub
, awoke Nil and Nether and brought them to the ridge overlooking the next day's battlefield. From there they observed the spirits of the land, Pormqual's fallen, and the fallen Malazans and Wickans of the Chain of Dogs destroy the
Dogslayers
in their trenches. They later told the Adjunct that their grief had blinded them to the spirits of the fallen that had joined with the army as it retraced Coltaine's steps.
In
The Bonehunters
After the Battle of Raraku, Leoman led the Army of the Apocalypse westward towards
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. In the
Lato Odhan
, Nil and Nether conducted a ritual to travel beyond
Hood's Gate
seeking Wickans who had died during the
Chain of Dogs
. The effort was similar to the magic of the
Tanno
Spiritwalkers
and one they had performed before. According to
Bottle
, the ritual was relatively safe as the pair were pretty sneaky and unlikely to attract attention.
But the mage was forced to chase after them and found Nil and Nether confronted by an angry lich. The lich screamed and tossed them about before disappearing. Nil revealed that the angry spirit was their
mother
. She had scolded Nil, telling him to "stop moping and grow up", while advising Nether to "take a husband and get pregnant."
Before they could leave Hood's Realm they were approached by the ghost of
Bult
with a dozen
Wickan cattle-dogs
. The warrior warned "we don't belong here" before advising Nether to "get married and have babies". Nether was not amused.
At the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
, Nil and Nether stood at Adjunct Tavore's side observing the battle.
They were powerless to stop the firestorm unleashed by Leoman because the earth spirits were trapped and dying by the flames just as the Malazan army was. But they sensed something of great power was about to be born. Nether was the first to identify it as
Sinn
, an unrealised
High Mage
. Sinn's efforts, along with the army's gathered witches and warlocks, were enough to free hundreds from the fire.
Afterwards, they told the Adjunct that Leoman had been spirited away by the
Queen of Dreams
. When Nil reported that
Poliel
's plague was at the army's heels, the Adjunct asked Nether what Poliel's goal was. Nether stated it was hopeless to fathom the mind of a
goddess
.
The 14th Army hurriedly marched to the shore of the
Kokakal Sea
to board
Admiral
Nok
's
transports
and return to
Quon Tali
. The entire fleet soon faced destruction at the hands of the
Third Edur Imperial Fleet
but for the intervention of Bottle and the
Eres'al
. Nil teased his sister for her romantic interest in the young mage, and both agreed to keep the Eres'al's involvement a secret.
Adjunct Tavore's fleet was redirected to
Malaz City
by order of Empress
Laseen
so that she and the Empress could meet in
Mock's Hold
. The Adjunct soon discovered that the Empress had reached a political settlement with
Mallick Rel
and
Korbolo Dom
that would raise both men to power while condemning the Wickans and Khundryl Burned Tears as scapegoats for the Empire's failures in Seven Cities. Mallick specifically called for
Pearl
to send his
Claws
to kill Nil and Nether. Nil and Nether had remained aboard Tavore's docked flagship, the
Froth Wolf
, while
Balm
, Fiddler, and Gesler's squads organised to defend it against an angry mob. During the fighting on the docks, both Nil and Nether honoured the soldiers defending them with a bow.
Tavore refused to deliver her loyal troops up to slaughter and instead took the entire army renegade. She relieved Nil, Nether,
Temul
, and the other Wickans from duty so that they could return to their homeland and defend it from the planned Malazan pogrom. Nether sought out Bottle and told the dumbfounded mage to return to her when his task was done.
Shadowthrone
lamented the ill treatment of his loyal Wickans with
Tayschrenn
. But the
High Mage
argued that with Nil and Nether, the Wickans were not as vulnerable as he feared.
In
Return of the Crimson Guard
An older and more seasoned teen Nether returned home to the
Wickan Plains
with Nil to lead their people during the Malazan civil war. Rising tensions between Wickans and Malazan settlers led to murder and violence. Over seventy Wickan elders and children took shelter at the Malazan border fort commanded by Lieutenant
Rillish Jal Keth
before a settler mob surrounded and besieged it. Rillish refused to turn the Wickans over to the mob, and after several weeks the fort fell. Only a suicidal ritual conducted by the Wickan elders to open a magic gateway allowed the soldiers and children to escape.
The Wickan children led the soldiers to the sacred Golden Hills where they were found by Nil and Nether. They revealed that one of the rescued children was Coltaine reborn, and they were determined to take advantage of the chaos Malazan civil war to invade Unta province and force a renegotiation of the Wickan treaties. A moved Rillish joined them as their military adviser.
While sacking
D'Avig
, Nether and Rillish chased the sorcerer
Dol D'Avig
through the
warrens
ultimately arriving in the
Imperial Warren
. Rillish faced
Ragman
, who quickly departed, apparently sensing Nether and saying, "Not who I was expecting. No, not yet, I think."
After taking
Fortress Jurda
, Nil and Nether decided they instead needed to make a more notable and lasting effort to strengthen their bargaining position.
The sorcerers, Rillish, and a force of one thousand Wickans travelled by
warren
to
Li Heng
where they proved to be the decisive factor in the Empire's victory over the
Crimson Guard
at the
Battle of the Plains
.
When the mad mage
Yathengar
opened a
Chaos
rent
upon the field, Nil and Nether joined the
Crimson Guard
and Malazan forces that attempted to close it. They only succeeded in getting wounded and were dragged out of harm's way by the disapproving Wickan mage
Su
, the elder cousin of their grandmother.
Su, with Nil and Nether in tow, later confronted new Emperor
Mallick Rel
and appeared to gain Imperial concessions regarding the Wickan lands.
Quotes
Nil
: "
The locals believe Coltaine ascended, Nether. The new Patron of Crows—
"
Nether
: "
Fools. Wickans do not ascend. We just… reiterate.
"
―Nether and Nil
