Nil
Biographical information
Race
Human
(
Wickan
)
Gender
Male
Family
Nether
(twin sister)
Social information
Affiliation
Malazan Empire
Malaz 7th Army
Occupation(s)
Warlock
Nil
was a
Wickan
warlock
and the twin brother of
Nether
. He had long unkempt black hair,
and spoke with a reedy voice.
He sometimes carried a feather-bedecked, knobbed club.
In
Deadhouse Gates
Nil was around nine or ten years old
when he served in
Sormo E'nath
's cadre of mages.  He traveled to
Hissar
on
Seven Cities
to support
Coltaine
, the newly appointed Wickan
Fist
of the
Malaz 7th Army
.  When the
Whirlwind
rebellion drove the Fist out of Hissar, he became one of Coltaine's
Chain of Dogs
.
Nil joyfully summoned a horde of undead warriors to battle
Kamist Reloe
's army of the
Apocalypse
at the
Battle of Sekala Crossing
. Then, once the River
Sekala
had been safely forded, Nil, Nether, and Sormo unleashed the spirits of the land to destroy the
Semk
tribal god.
Later Nil and another
young warlock
led a mission to assassinate a
Tithansi Warleader
with
Duiker
,
Lull
, and a squad of
Sialk Marines
only to discover he was the
Semk godling
returned. The other warlock was killed, while Nil was stricken unconscious and had to be brought back to camp on a travois.
The Ritual by
Dejan Delic
At the
Battle of Gelor Ridge
he and Nether performed a
ritual
on the horses of the
Foolish Dog
Clan which allowed them to charge uphill at an unnaturally high speed and strike Reloe's elite infantry legions.
Afterwards, the twins' skin was pale, their hands were stained black, and they were confined to bed for days.
When the Fist bloodied the near-
Ascendant
Gesler
's nose at Vathar Crossing, both Nil and Nether gasped in recognition that Coltaine himself was on the path to Ascendency.
Sormo was killed at the
Battle of Vathar Crossing
, leaving Nil and Nether the army's sole remaining warlocks.
After the
Battle of Sanimon
, Coltaine sent the twins and the refugees ahead of the army along with Duiker and an escort of Wickan youths. They arrived at the gates of
Aren
without major incident.
Nil and Nether stood safely on the walls of Aren as Coltaine and the last of his soldiers were cut down on the plain below. Nil collapsed in Nether's arms and then lay on the ground, curled and motionless in grief.
In
House of Chains
Both Nil and Nether were broken by their experience on the Chain of Dogs.  Nil allowed his deer-hide tunic to become scarred and worn, and both twins went about dirty and barefoot.
When
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
arrived in Aren with the
Malaz 14th Army
, neither wanted to accompany the punitive expedition against the
Army of the Whirlwind
.  Their magic was no longer strong.  They could speak to spirits, but no longer compel them.  But as the Adjunct had few mages, she refused to let them return home, holding them to Coltaine's last command and advising them to find a way to awaken the warlock spirits inside themselves.
As the army retraced the Chain of Dogs' steps in reverse, Nil and Nether spent their time attempting to communicate with the spirit of Sormo E'nath.
Fiddler
found the two facing each other over a bronze bowl near the site of
Vathar Crossing
.  A swarm of yellow butterflies engulfed the
Bridgeburner
, speaking into his ear.  Nil and Nether were heartbroken that the warlock's only contact had been with a stranger, and they demanded to know if Sormo had a message for them.  Fiddler concluded that the presence he felt was not Sormo's.
By the time the army arrived at
Raraku
, Nil had grown taller and more feral in appearance with wild, unbraided hair.  He dressed only in a loincloth and green and black body-paint.
He and his sister confirmed that the Adjunct was right to suspect that the warrior spirits of the desert resisted the
Whirlwind Goddess
' attempt to feed on the land's memories.
On the eve of the
Battle of Raraku
, the boy,
Grub
, awoke Nil and Nether and brought them to the ridge overlooking the next day's battlefield.  From there they observed the spirits of the land, Pormqual's fallen, and the fallen Malazans and Wickans of the Chain of Dogs destroy the
Dogslayers
in their trenches.  They later told the Adjunct that their grief had blinded them to the spirits of the fallen that had joined with the army as it retraced Coltaine's steps.  Nil also told her that Fist
Gamet
had joined the spirits in their attack.
In
The Bonehunters
After the Battle of Raraku, Leoman led the Army of the Apocalypse westward towards
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. In the
Lato Odhan
, Nil and Nether conducted a ritual to travel beyond
Hood's Gate
seeking Wickans who had died during the
Chain of Dogs
.  The effort was similar to the magic of the
Tanno
Spiritwalkers
and one they had performed before.  According to
Bottle
, the ritual was relatively safe as the pair were pretty sneaky and unlikely to attract attention.
But the mage was forced to chase after them and found Nil and Nether confronted by an angry lich.  The lich screamed and tossed them about before disappearing.  Nil revealed that the angry spirit was their
mother
.  She had scolded Nil, telling him to "stop moping and grow up", while advising Nether to "take a husband and get pregnant."
Before they could leave Hood's Realm they were approached by the ghost of
Bult
with a dozen
Wickan cattle-dogs
.  The warrior warned "we don't belong here".
At the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
, Nil and Nether stood at Adjunct Tavore's side observing the battle.
They were powerless to stop the firestorm unleashed by Leoman because the earth spirits were trapped and dying by the flames just as the Malazan army was.  But they sensed something of great power was about to be born.  Nether was the first to identify it as
Sinn
, an unrealised
High Mage
.  Sinn's efforts, along with the army's gathered witches and warlocks, were enough to free hundreds from the fire.
Afterwards, Nil was exhausted by the sorcery he had grown to hate.  He told the Adjunct that Leoman had been spirited away by the
Queen of Dreams
and that the land's spirits, driven insane by agony, cursed the Malazans for the crimes of Y'Ghatan.  He declared that Y'Ghatan would never rise again and both Wickans reported that
Poliel
's plague was at the army's heels.
The 14th Army hurriedly marched to the shore of the
Kokakal Sea
to board

Nok
's

and return to

. The entire fleet soon faced destruction at the hands of the

Tavore refused to deliver her loyal troops up to slaughter and instead took the entire army renegade. She relieved Nil, Nether,
Temul

Wickan Plains

Rillish Jal Keth

Coltaine
reborn, and they were determined to take advantage of the chaos Malazan civil war to invade Unta province and force a renegotiation of the Wickan treaties. A moved Rillish joined them as their military adviser.

D'Avig
and
Fortress Jurda

PAGE: Nose Stream
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters

======================================================================

Nose Stream
was a
sergeant
in the
Bonehunters
in
Hedge
's squad of
New Bridgeburners
. He was recruited from
Letheras
and received his new name from
Master Sergeant Pores
.
In
Dust of Dreams
Nose Stream and thirty-nine other
Letherii
recruits were snatched up by
Bavedict
to join Hedge's New Bridgeburners. Before that Master Sergeant Pores had them tied to several existing squads, who weren't too pleased about it. Nose Stream and
Sunrise
became the first sergeants, with
Rumjugs
and
Sweetlard
as their corporals.
In
The Crippled God
Nose Stream isn't mentioned again after the battle with the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
. Due to the promotion of
Rumjugs
and
Sweetlard
to sergeant it can be assumed, that he didn't survive the battle.

PAGE: Ordinary Grey

Sergeant
Ordinary Grey
was a regular in the
Bonehunters
(formerly known as the Malazan 14th Army).  When Sergeant
Gaunt-Eyes
' own squad had tried to murder him, Ordinary Grey along with
Could Howl
had held them off and cut them down.  Grey stood up for the sergeant because Gaunt-Eye had long ago shown him kindness in the Holy Desert of
Raraku
.
In
The Crippled God
Tavore Paran
named Ordinary Grey in the
speech
when she addressed the Regulars facing the
Forkrul Assail
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Pella
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Pella
======================================================================

Pella
was a
Malazan
soldier garrisoned at
Skullcup
, an
Otataral mining
camp.
He was described as a young man, young enough to be referred to as 'the boy'.
Pella had calluses ridging the index finger and thumb of his sword hand.
In
Deadhouse Gates
Pella was guarding Nearlight's Gate in Skullcup when
Beneth
and
Felisin Paran
approached. Speaking with them, he quoted
Kellanved
from Duiker's
Imperial Campaigns
and recommended that Felisin should find someone who could tell her the remainder of the quote.
Two weeks later, Pella asked Felisin if she had found someone but she did not remember the conversation. He ignored her offer of sharing her bed and went off to find
Heboric
.
It transpired that Pella worked at the behest of
Duiker
to help
Baudin
, Heboric, and Felisin Paran escape the camp on the night of the
Whirlwind
uprising. He stayed behind to help the other soldiers defend against Captain
Gunnip
's mutinous
Dosin Pali
guards.
In
House of Chains
One of the few to escape the rebellion at Skullcup, Pella and some fellow soldiers made their way to Dosin Pali over four nights. A Malazan trader ship took them eventually on to
Aren
.
Pella was then integrated into the
Malaz 14th Army
where he was part of
Gesler
's 5th squad, 9th Company in the
8th Legion
.
Before the army left Aren, Pella was questioned by
Lostara Yil
regarding Felisin Paran's time at Skullcup.  He admitted to helping her and her companions escape.
During the army's march on
Raraku
,
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
laid an ambush for
Leoman
and his desert raiders.
Fist
Gamet
was seriously injured in the attack, and Pella aided Gesler in carrying the wounded man to safety.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
, Leoman led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward towards
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed.  Adjunct Tavore wanted to send some of her people ahead to reach the city first, so she chose Gesler's squad (including Pella) to accompany
Quick Ben
and
Kalam Mekhar
.  The group travelled via the
Imperial Warren
, but due to the problems with the Warrens travel was difficult and confusing.
The sudden appearance of at least a dozen
K'Chain Che'Malle
Skykeeps
in the air above led Quick Ben to immediately cancel the plan.  He brought the group back to the Malazan world to report the news to the Adjunct.
In the lead up to the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
, Pella decided to stick close to
Truth
, who he considered "too wide-eyed for all this."
Adjunct Tavore launched the battle by breaching the city's walls with
Sappers
.  Upon hearing the
munitions
go off, Pella questioned his decision to join the
marines
or even soldiery, thinking he should have run after Skullcup.
First into the city were the Malazan marines, followed quickly by the
Heavy infantry
. Barely a street in and fearing an ambush, Gesler called for backup while Pella and Truth scanned the windows above with their
crossbows
. Pella dismissed a momentary rustle in a high window as a trick of the wind while sappers and heavies entered the buildings around them.  Amidst the sound of an ambush and munitions fire inside, an archer from above put an arrow into Pella's forehead.  He died thinking of his mother.
History
Pella grew up in a slum.  When he was a boy, he had skinned his knees while playing in a filthy cobblestoned alley.  His mother had been so afraid of him catching disease that she spent their savings on a healer.  Afterwards, Pella carried the guilt that the money had been meant for his mother's dream of moving them to a better part of the slum.

======================================================================
PAGE: Pores
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Pores
======================================================================

Aramstos Pores
Biographical information
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Social information
Affiliation
Malazan Empire
Ashok Regiment
Bonehunters
Occupation(s)
Soldier
Rank
Lieutenant
"
It's not as if I'm afraid of war. It's the chaos I don't like.
"
―Aramstos Pores
Lieutenant
Aramstos Pores
directly reported to
Captain Kindly
, first in the 2nd Company of the
Ashok Regiment
,
and then later in the
Bonehunters
. He and his captain had a comically adversarial relationship.
Ruthan Gudd
described Pores as a match for Kindly's wits and an exception to the rule which said that lieutenants were usually "either ambitious backstabbers or butt-licking fools".
In
House of Chains
Pores served under Kindly's command at the
Malazan
garrison in
Silver Lake
when
Karsa Orlong
,
Bairoth Gild
, and
Delum Thord
attacked the town.
As a response to rumours of rebellion on
Seven Cities
, Kindly's regiment was recalled back from Genabackis. They escorted prisoners Karsa and
Torvald Nom
as far as the port of
Tanys
where they took a different ship across the
Malyn Sea
.
The Ashok Regiment was then presumably posted in
Ehrlitan
when the
Whirlwind
rebellion began.
Several hundred Malazans, including the Ashok Regiment, fled from Ehrlitan,
G'danisban
, and
Pan'potsun
to hole up in the cliff-side fortress of
B'ridys
.
There Kindly and Pores fell down a well and were presumed drowned.
They actually managed to escape the
creature
at the bottom of the well only to later be captured and imprisoned in
Raraku
by
Korbolo Dom
's
Dogslayers
.
They were set free by
Bridgeburner
ghosts on the eve of the
confrontation
between
Sha'ik
and
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
and were then brought to the camp of the
Malaz 14th Army
by
Fist
Tene Baralta
and his men.
In
The Bonehunters
Pores by
Dejan Delic
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Keneb
was promoted to Fist and Kindly temporarily replaced him as captain of the
8th Legion
's 9th Company in the
Malaz 14th Army
.  Pores continued to serve Kindly as his lieutenant.
Leoman
led the Army of the Apocalypse westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed.  About the time the 14th Army arrived at
Y'Ghatan
, Kindly was replaced by
Faradan Sort
and both Kindly and Pores were reassigned to another company.
Pores briefly reminisced about his old squad (
Ebron
,
Limp
,
Bell
, and
Sinn
) before concluding he did not miss them that much after all.
At the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
, Pores was caught in the firestorm and the fingers of his shield hand were fused together.  Kindly found him recovering in the hospital tent and chastised him for loafing. The 14th Army then made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
. Three days west of Y'Ghatan Pores led a patrol that was ambushed by starving bandits and he took a
crossbow
quarrel clean through his upper left arm and sword-slash deep enough above the right knee to sever muscle down to the bone.  Healers were able to roughly knit together his wounds, but the pain was excruciating.  Kindly physically dragged him off a convalescent wagon to make room for soldiers with "real injuries" and placed him in charge of picket duty.
Pores thought his captain was insane.
Later, Pores was the first to spot the odd behaviour of the
Wickan cattle-dogs
who ran out of camp to meet the returning
Fiddler
and the other missing survivors of Y'Ghatan. He stole Adjunct Tavore's horse to investigate, then raced back into camp to order water and healers brought up to aid them.
The army embarked aboard
Admiral
Nok
's ships to return to
Quon Tali
.
At
Malaz City
, Kindly's troops remained on their ships in the harbour while the Adjunct went ashore to meet Empress
Laseen
in
Mock's Hold
. Fighting broke out on the pier between the citizens of Malaz City and the 14th soldiers guarding the Adjunct's
flagship
. Kindly rejected Pores' request to send aid, saying he would be happy to promote
Hanfeno
in the Lieutenant's place while
Senny
took bets on whether Pores could survive swimming to shore across the shark-filled harbour.
In
Reaper's Gale
After Adjunct Tavore's clash with the Empress at Malaz City she took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, spreading Fist Keneb's
marines
in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast and burning their
transport vessels
behind them. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
The rest of the Adjunct's fleet gathered at
Second Maiden Fort
where Tavore hired the pirate,
Shurq Elalle
, to guide them to the mouth of the
Lether River
leading to Letheras.
Aboard ship, Pores still affected a limp from his injuries at Y'Ghatan in what he realised was a pathetic attempt at eliciting sympathy from Captain Kindly. Kindly only found it annoying and warned him to stop it unless he wanted the captain to shatter his leg with a billy club. When Kindly caught Pores looking across the waves admiring the voluptuous
Masan Gilani
aboard the nearby
Silanda
, he reprimanded the lieutenant and ordered him to draw up papers to place Gilani on report for being out of uniform. Before Pores could even make it back to his cabin to begin the report, Kindly followed up behind to oversee his penmanship. Then he tasked Pores with cleaning the new turtleshell combs the captain had acquired from the
Shake
at Second Maiden Fort.
The Adjunct's fleet made landfall near Letheras and defeated the city's
Imperial Brigade
with Kindly leading Fist
Blistig
's infantry.
Meanwhile, Keneb's marines secretly entered the city to secure its western gate to allow the rest of the army entrance.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
After Pores was caught masquerading as
Kindly
to several soldiers, Kindly promoted Pores "sideways" to the rank of
Master Sergeant
thinking it a punishment.
He was lumbered with several 'green'
Letherii
recruits which he was ordered to train, but got out of doing it as
Hedge
commandeered the soldiers for his new Bridgeburners, leaving Pores to his own devices.
In
The Crippled God
Pores, in his role as unofficial 'Quartermaster', had his nose broken by someone, resulting in black eyes.
Pores was commanded by
Fist
Blistig
to secretly hold a number of water barrels for him in reserve, as the Bonehunters commenced their journey across the
Glass Desert
.
Setting the barrels aside and having notified Kindly of the situation, Pores later opened them under Adjunct Tavore's direct command in order to slake the thirst of the
Snake
, a group of refugee children.
Later, when the water for the army had just about run out, Pores was purposely isolated from the Bonehunters and subsequently stabbed by Blistig in order for the latter not only to get access to 'his' water barrels, but so as to also hide what he had done.
Kindly, having been informed of the vicious attack on Pores by Sergeant
Balm
, and that
Ruthan Gudd
had determined that blood found on Blistig's knife belonged to Pores, decided to take matters into his own hands in order to avenge the Lieutenant.
Pores' life was only barely saved by 'heroic' emergency surgery performed by
Deadsmell
, with the unexpected aid of a couple of
The Unbound
T'lan Imass
, who were now traveling with the army.
Quotes
"
There were times, he reflected morosely, when he wanted to kill Captain Kindly.
"
―Pores

======================================================================
PAGE: Pravalak Rim
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Pravalak_Rim
======================================================================

Pravalak Rim
[PRA-vuh-lak RIM] was
Corporal
of
Sinter
's 4th squad,
8th Legion
, 3rd Company of the
Bonehunters
. The youngest son in his family, he was a country boy who had been lured into the
Malazan Military
by a beautiful, middle-aged
Dal Honese
recruiter.
"
Corporal Pravalak Rim was a haunted man. Born in a northern province of
Gris
to poor farmers, he had seen nothing of the world for most of his life, until the day a
marine
recruiter had come through the nearby village on the very day Pravalak was there with his older brothers, all of whom sneered at the marine on their way to the tavern. But Pravalak himself, well, he had stared in disbelief. His first sight of someone from
Dal Hon
. She had been big and round and though she was decades older than him and her hair had gone grey he could see how she had been beautiful and indeed, to his eyes, she still was.
"
―Pravalak Rim's background
That day he had simultaneously lost his virginity and been inducted into the army. Although his first great love affair only lasted as long the recruiter's wagon took to get to the next town, he soon found plenty of other Dal Hon women in the army to admire. The latest was
Kisswhere
, who had rejected him and with whom he was utterly smitten. Sinter, Kisswhere's sister, encouraged him to continue the pursuit, assuring him her sister was coming around.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the
marines
in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Sinter's squad, along with
Badan Gruk
's 5th and
Primly
's 10th squads, landed furthest south of all the marines. Remaining together, they saw little resistance moving east and soon reached a river. Rather than slog through through waist-deep swamp muck, they stole a fisher boat and sailed upriver. They made excellent time until running into a Letherii galley in the night. Kisswhere and Sinter were lost in the water during a discharge of
Moranth munitions
. Forced ashore, they were pursued day and night, using up their mages dodging and ducking enemy attacks. Pravalak Rim had seen Kisswhere's hand disappear under the water and he was devastated by her loss. He wished to die himself even as he took command of Sinster's squad with Primly's encouragement.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the
Malazan
invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
The marines further north saw intense action, and as they neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and their munition supplies dwindled.
Hellian
and
Urb
's squads earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler
and
Gesler
's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
Three days after leaving the river, Sinter, Primly, and Badan Gruk's squads came upon the overwhelmed Malazans. Badan Gruk, Primly, and Corporal
Hunt
met to discuss what to do without inviting Pravalak Rim to their discussion. Badan Gruk thought to pass around the embattled marines, but Primly and Corporal Hunt argued that their squads were ready to fight. The three squads turned the tide of battle turned the tide of battle with their fresh supply of munitions. The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by
Fist
Keneb
.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, the seized the city's western gate to allow the rest of the army entrance.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
(Information needed)
In
The Crippled God
Rim had to have his weapon arm amputated following the battle against the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
.

Primly
was the
Quon Talian
sergeant
of the 10th squad,
8th Legion
, 3rd Company of the
Bonehunters
. He was quite young and so did not have much of a beard on his long ascetic face.
He had been a Quon noble, but had committed some act that left him disowned and possibly on the run.
During his time in the army he had left whatever highborn airs he possessed behind.
Badan Gruk
thought Primly's face soured whenever anyone spoke to him.
Members of Primly's squad
Hunt
, corporal
Drawfirst
, heavy infantry
Masker
, heavy infantry
Mulvan Dreader
, mage
Neller
, sapper
Skulldeath
, marine
Note: In the
Reaper's Gale
Dramatis Personae
the
heavy
Lookback
is listed as part of 4th squad and the heavy
Drawfirst
as part of Primly's 10th squad. But the text of the book refers to Lookback as the last remaining heavy in the 10th, suggesting their squads should be reversed.
It is unclear which source is correct.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the
marines
in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Primly's squad, along with
Sinter
's 4th and Badan Gruk's 5th squads, landed furthest south of all the marines. Remaining together, they saw little resistance moving east and soon reached a river. Rather than slog through through waist-deep swamp muck, they stole a fisher boat and sailed upriver. They made excellent time until running into a Letherii galley in the night.
Kisswhere
and Sinter were lost in the water during a discharge of
Moranth munitions
. Forced ashore, they were pursued day and night, using up their mages dodging and ducking enemy attacks. Somewhere along the way
Masker
was also lost, leaving Primly with only one heavy.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the
Malazan
invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
The marines further north saw intense action, and as they neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and their munition supplies dwindled.
Hellian
and
Urb
's squads earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler
and
Gesler
's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
Three days after leaving the river, Primly, Sinter, and Badan Gruk's squads came upon the overwhelmed Malazans. Badan Gruk immediately thought to pass around them, but Primly and Corporal
Hunt
argued that their squads were ready to fight. The three squads turned the tide of battle with their fresh supply of munitions. The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by
Fist
Keneb
.
Primly was forced to intervene when
Hellian
and
Skulldeath
's mutual sexual attraction became too public.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, the seized the city's western gate to allow the rest of the army entrance.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
In
Dust of Dreams
(Information needed)
In
The Crippled God
It was revealed that Primly and most of his squad died in the battle against the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Rackle
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Rackle
======================================================================

Rackle
was a soldier in the
Bonehunters
under the direct command of
Fist
Blistig
.
In
The Crippled God
Rackle was a known trouble-maker.  He, along with nine others, including
Bester
and
Stull
, were widely known as "Fist Blistig's gang of thugs".
After the Bonehunters had begun their transverse of the
Glass Desert
on their way to
Kolanse
, Blistig ordered Lieutenant 'Quartermaster'
Pores
to mark and secretly set aside a number of barrels of water for his eventual personal use and that of his gang of accomplices, including Rackle, Bester and Stull.
In time, the Army's water supply became vanishingly scarce and tightly rationed. One night, Rackle, Bester and Stull were picked by Blistig to help him retrieve the marked water barrels from the Quartermaster's wagon.
In order to obtain access to the barrels, both Pores and his clerk,
Shorthand
, needed to be eliminated. Rackle, accompanied by Bester and Stull, proceeded to break Shorthand's skull with a blow from a mace to the side of his head. Blistig, himself, took care of Pores, stabbing him with a knife.
Bester and Stull then hid in the darkness with stolen crossbows and quarrels to set up an ambush for Sergeant
Balm
's squad of marines, whose duty it was to guard the wagon and its contents that night. The ambush failed, however, and Rackle was killed by
Widdershins
, while Bester and Stull disappeared into the ranks of the 'Regulars'.

======================================================================
PAGE: Ramp
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Ramp
======================================================================

Ramp
was a 12th squad
medium infantryman
of the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
. He served under
Sergeant
Thom Tissy
.
In
House of Chains
Ramp was part of
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
's punitive expedition against the
Army of the Apocalypse
.  On the road from
Aren
to
Raraku
, he, Thom Tissy,
Tulip
, and
Able
had done their share of the fighting, and their names were well known amongst the other soldiers in the legion.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the Army of the Apocalypse westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. Adjunct Tavore launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the
Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the
heavy
and medium infantry.
Barely a street in and fearing an ambush, Sergeant
Gesler
called up
Moak
's squad as well as
Tugg
's heavies and Thom Tissy's newly designated sappers to clear the surrounding buildings. In the fighting that followed, the poorly trained Able,
Gupp
, and
Jump
misfired their
munitions
killing Moak's entire squad and themselves. Thom Tissy kept his head and charged forward with Ramp and Tulip to support Tugg's heavies.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap. The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. Thom Tissy's squad and a mixed group of survivors from Gesler's,
Fiddler
's,
Hellian
's, and
Balm
's squads were driven by the fires to the Temple of the
Queen of Dreams
.  Ramp was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city. They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
.
After escaping the city, Ramp and the other survivors eventually caught up to the 14th Army west of
Sotka
as it embarked on
Admiral
Nok
's Malazan Imperial Fleet to return to
Quon Tali
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Ramp was now a
Heavy
in Thom Tissy's 12th Squad, which was composed of Corporal
Tulip
,
Jibb
,
Gullstream
,
Mudslinger
, and
Bellig Harn
.
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Fist
Keneb
followed in their wake with six squads of marines, including Tissy's 12th squad.
Once the marines began engaging with the enemy, Keneb had difficulty maintaining contact with his lead elements. Tissy told Keneb that he and the others in the squad understood his anxiety at following impossible orders under difficult conditions. The Fist called him presumptuous and told him to tell his squad to stop theorising.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
As the marines neared Letheras fighting became more desperate, and a large force of Edur stood between Keneb's troops and the forward marines. Thom Tissy heartened the Fist by claiming his troops were ready for a hard fight. They fought their way to a village where all the remaining squads had converged before continuing on together to the capital.
Thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing them towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Thom Tissy's squad was among those sent to secure the city's western gate from the inside to allow the main army entrance into the city. City Garrison soldiers tried to retake the gate in bloody fighting, but Tissy's squad held on long enough for
Balm
's squad, and then others, to arrive.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
Trivia
Although included in the
Dramatis Personae
of
Reaper's Gale
, Ramp was not mentioned by name anywhere in the text of the novel.

======================================================================
PAGE: Reem
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Reem
======================================================================

Bottle
: "
What are they fighting over?
"
Toles
: "
It's very simple.  Two squads, marching in step, one behind the other, then the other in front of the one that had been in front beforehand, proving the mythical camaraderie to be no more than some epic instigator of bad poetry and bawdy songs designed to appease lowbrows, in short, a lie. Culminating at the last in this disreputable display of animal instincts—
"
Reem
: "
Saltlick bit Shortnose's ear off.
"
―Reem cuts to the chase
Corporal
Reem
served under
Sergeant
Sobelone
in the
Heavy infantry
of the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. Once the 14th Army reached the city's outskirts, an impromptu wrestling match broke out between
Saltlick
and
Shortnose
with the rest of Sobelone and
Tugg
's squads watching and placing bets.
Bottle
asked
Toles
for an explanation, but before the verbose soldier could complete his account, Reem offered his own pithy report.
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the heavy and
medium infantry
.  Once inside the city, the Malazans immediately came under attack from hidden archers and warriors. Sobelone and
Toles
were killed in one such ambush. Reem,
Hanno
, and the other survivors of Sobelone's squad were rallied by Sergeant
Hellian
, who orchestrated a counterattack against their ambushers using
smokers
.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap. The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. Reem's and Hellian's squads joined a mixed group of survivors from
Cord
's,
Fiddler
's, and
Borduke
's squads fleeing the flames to the Temple of the
Queen of Dreams
. Reem was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city. They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
.
Unaware that any had survived, the 14th Army made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
.
Faradan Sort
and
Sinn
remained behind and discovered the survivors as they crawled from the wreckage.
Reem and the others made the long march west, finally catching up to the army on the coast.
Nok's fleet returned the army to
Malaz City
where the Adjunct met with Empress
Laseen
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress Laseen at Malaz City and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Fist
Keneb
followed in their wake with six squads of marines, while Faradan Sort and
Beak
attempted to keep lines of communication open between both groups.
Reem was made a corporal in Urb's 13th squad.
Urb's squad was paired with Hellian's for the landings and the two squads remained together with
Bowl
and
Balgrid
using their magic to cover their tracks.
After defeating a troop of Edur at
Boaral Keep
they acquired mounts at Hellian's suggestion and pushed hard inland for the capital, fighting from tavern to tavern.
The two squads began taking trophies of ear and fingers and tying them to their belts.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
When the two squads ambushed sixteen Letherii and four Edur mounted on horseback with
Crossbows
and
Moranth munitions
, the Letherii veterans recovered more quickly than expected and
Hanno
was killed. Reem lost two fingers on his left hand because of a bad block with his shield.
In the aftermath, Saltlick and Reem got to talking of how much they missed their former comrade,
Masan Gilani
. Reem insisted she had requested a transfer to
Balm
's squad because she was so attracted to Urb she could not think straight. When the inebriated Hellian tried to bed a terrified Urb, the corporal speculated that the noise of their lovemaking might have moved a frustrated Gilani to settle for himself or one of the other soldiers. An exasperated Balgrid wondered where Reem's sudden runaway mouth came from, remarking that the corporal was better being silent and mysterious. Reem said he just felt like talking.
As the marines neared Letheras fighting became more desperate, although Hellian earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler and
Gesler
's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
The Edur were repelled by the arrival of
Badan Gruk
,
Sinter
, and
Primly
's fresh squads.
The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by Fist Keneb.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under Beak's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Urb, Hellian, Fiddler, and Gesler's squads were sent into the city to cause trouble while the remaining marines opened the city's west gate to Tavore's infantry. Hellian's squad quickly disappeared into a local tavern and Urb was tasked with finding them.
After the main force of Malazans entered the city, the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.

======================================================================
PAGE: Reliko
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Reliko
======================================================================

Reliko
was a
Dal Honese
heavy
in
Badan Gruk
's 5th squad in the
Bonehunters
'
8th Legion
, Third Company. He was described as being short, with an ebon-skinned face
and no neck to speak of.
Being half a head shorter than his already small
sergeant
, Reliko was reported by
Braven Tooth
to be the smallest heavy infantryman in the history of the
Malazan Empire
.
He kept an eye on squad mate
Vastly Blank
, making sure the thickheaded heavy did not misplace his weapon or forget who the enemy was.
He carried a shortsword and shield.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the Bonehunters rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the
marines
in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the
Letherii
countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a mage responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Badan Gruk's squad, along with
Sinter
's 4th and
Primly
's 10th squads, landed furthest south of all the marines. Remaining together, they saw little resistance moving east and soon reached a river. Rather than slog through through waist-deep swamp muck, they stole a fisher boat and sailed upriver. They made excellent time until running into a Letherii galley in the night.
Kisswhere
and Sinter were lost in the water during a discharge of
Moranth munitions
. Forced ashore, they were pursued day and night, using up their mages dodging and ducking enemy attacks. On the first night, Badan Gruk lost his corporal after the man fell down an abandoned well shaft and broke his neck. Badan Gruk chose
Ruffle
to take his place. Somewhere along the way the
Heavy
,
Masker
, was also lost, but Badan Gruk,
Skulldeath
, and others had yet to draw blood.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the
Malazan
invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
The marines further north saw intense action, and as they neared Letheras fighting became more desperate and their munition supplies dwindled.
Hellian
and
Urb
's squads earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler
and
Gesler
's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
Three days after leaving the river, Badan Gruk, Sinter, and Primly's squads came upon the overwhelmed Malazans and turned the battle with their fresh supply of munitions. The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by
Fist
Keneb
.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under
Beak
's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Badan Gruk's squad was among those sent to secure the city's western gate from the inside to allow the main army entrance into the city. City Garrison soldiers tried to retake the gate in bloody fighting. Reliko suffered a severed tendon in the arm that rolled up under the skin, but Badan Gruk's squad held on long enough for he and Vastly Blank to greet Adjunct Tavore and her group of cavalry when they arrived.
Soon the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.

Dust of Dreams

In
The Crippled God

======================================================================
PAGE: Rib
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Rib
======================================================================

Rib
was a
corporal
in the Malazan
Bonehunters
. He was in the 18th squad under Sergeant
Gaunt-Eye
.
In
Dust of Dreams
During the investigation of destroyed tent of
Stormy
and
Gesler
, Rib took the reins of Fist
Keneb's
horse and gave him his assessment of the situation. Sergeant
Gaunt-Eye
was send to disperse the gawking soldiers. In Rib's opinion, his sergeant didn't need any help for that, because he was the meanest sergeant he had ever met
.
In
The Crippled God
Sergeant
Gaunt-Eye
and Corporal Rib were the only survivors from their squad, after the battle with the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
. Gaunt-Eye conscripted the surviving members of the 10th squad,
Skulldeath
and
Drawfirst
, to join them in the 18th squad. Two soldiers from the 7th and two from the 9th Company's 5th squad were also conscripted to make up numbers
. Two of them were the heavies
Flashwit
and
Mayfly
.
Notes
Flashwit
described Corporal Rib as one-armed, after her conversation with Sergeant Gaunt-Eye
. This is the only mention of him missing an arm. While he could have lost his arm in the battle with the K'Chain Nah'ruk or even earlier, this might also be a mix-up by Steven Erikson with the similarly named
Corporal Rim
, who's weapon arm had to be amputated after the battle
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Rove
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Rove
======================================================================

Rove
was a member of
Sergeant
Moak
's
Medium infantry
squad in the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
Malaz 14th Army
.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. Upon reaching the outskirts of the city, Moak prepared a stew for his squad using a ripened fish he had carried for weeks.  When his squad all "got the squats", he blamed it on their weak stomachs while a true soldier like himself suffered only from belches that smelled of rotting fish guts.
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the
heavy
and medium infantry. Barely a street in and fearing an ambush, Sergeant
Gesler
called up Moak's squad as well as
Thom Tissy
's sappers and
Tugg
's heavies to clear the surrounding buildings. In the fighting that followed, the poorly trained sappers misfired their
munitions
. One shrieking sapper exited the building fully aflame.  As Moak's squad went to help him, the sapper's munitions satchel went off killing Rove and Moak's entire squad.

======================================================================
PAGE: Rumjugs
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Rumjugs
======================================================================

Corporal
Rumjugs
was one of
Hedge
's squad of
New Bridgeburners
. She was recruited, along with
Sweetlard
, from a brothel in
Letheras
.
She was described as an enormous, sweaty woman with black hair, small eyes, and full lips.
In
Dust of Dreams
Rumjugs, Sweetlard and thirty-eight other
Letherii
recruits were snatched up by
Bavedict
to join Hedge's New Bridgeburners. Before that, Master Sergeant Pores had them tied to several existing squads, who weren't too pleased about the new recruits.
Nose Stream
and
Sunrise
became the first sergeants, with Rumjugs and Sweetlard as their corporals. During the first meeting with their new commander, Rumjugs and Sweetlard convinced their sergeants that they should be the ones to talk with Hedge about moving the camp away from the latrine trench, as he was a man and would propably be nicer to them.
In
The Crippled God
After the battle with the
K'Chain Nah'ruk
, Rumjugs and Sweetlard were promoted to the rank of Sergeant by Hedge. Both were exhausted and in shock after the loss of many comrades. They were present when
Berrach
and his sons joined the New Bridgeburners as their cavalary. Hedge noticed that the two women were starting to feel a bit better afterwards.
Hedge believed she and Sweetlard had fallen in the battle against the
Forkrul Assail
, but she was merely unconscious from heat prostration.

Sad
was the squad
mage

======================================================================
PAGE: Saltlick
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Saltlick
======================================================================

Reem
: "
Saltlick bit Shortnose's ear off.
"
Bottle
: "
Oh. Is that what he's chewing?
"
Reem
: "
Yeah. taking his time with it, too.
"
―Reem and Bottle watch  Saltlick wrestle Shortnose
Saltlick
(also called 'Salty')
was a
heavy infantryman
in the 9th Company,
8th Legion
of the
14th Army
.  He was in either Sergeant
Sobelone
's or Sergeant
Tugg
's squad of heavy infantry.
He had a massive, round face with an expression that was usually fixed in a cow-like state of uninterested incomprehension.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed.  Once the 14th Army reached the city's outskirts, an impromptu wrestling match broke out between Saltlick and
Shortnose
after Saltlick bit Shortnose's ear off. The rest of Sobelone and Tugg's squads gathered around the two straining men, watching and placing bets. Shortnose's wife,
Hanno
, bet against her husband.  Saltlick seemed to take the battle in stride, taking his time chewing his opponent's severed ear.
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the heavy and
medium infantry
.  Once inside the city, the Malazans immediately came under attack from hidden archers and warriors. Sobelone and Tugg were killed in separate ambushes.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap. The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. Saltlick joined a mixed group of survivors from
Cord
's,
Fiddler
's,
Hellian
's, and
Borduke
's squads fleeing the flames to the Temple of the
Queen of Dreams
. Saltlick was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city. They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
.
Unaware that any had survived, the 14th Army made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
.
Faradan Sort
and
Sinn
remained behind and discovered the survivors as they crawled from the wreckage.
Captain
Sort reorganised the shattered soldiers, promoting
Urb
to sergeant and placing Saltlick in his newly created 13th squad.
The remaining officers chose
Masan Gilani
to take the group's one remaining horse and try to catch up to the 14th Army.  Gilani promised Saltlick her prized hook-blade should she not return.
Saltlick and the others made the long march west, finally catching up to the army on the coast.
Nok's fleet returned the army to
Malaz City
where the Adjunct met with Empress
Laseen
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress Laseen at Malaz City and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Fist
Keneb
followed in their wake with six squads of marines, while Faradan Sort and
Beak
attempted to keep lines of communication open between both groups.
Saltlick was made a heavy in Urb's 13th squad.
Urb's squad was paired with Hellian's for the landings and the two squads remained together with
Bowl
and
Balgrid
using their magic to cover their tracks.
After defeating a troop of Edur at
Boaral Keep
they acquired mounts at Hellian's suggestion and pushed hard inland for the capital, fighting from tavern to tavern.
The two squads began taking trophies of ear and fingers and tying them to their belts.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
When the two squads ambushed sixteen Letherii and four Edur mounted on horseback with
Crossbows
and
Moranth munitions
, the Letherii veterans recovered more quickly than expected and
Hanno
was killed. Saltlick was left unconscious and badly cut up until Balgrid worked on him with his magic.
As the marines neared Letheras fighting became more desperate, although Hellian earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler and Gesler's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
The Edur were repelled by the arrival of
Badan Gruk
,
Sinter
, and
Primly
's fresh squads, although Saltlick lost his left hand in the fighting.
The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by Fist Keneb.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under Beak's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Urb, Hellian, Fiddler, and Gesler's squads were sent into the city to cause trouble while the remaining marines opened the city's west gate to Tavore's infantry. Hellian's squad quickly disappeared into a local tavern and Urb was tasked with finding them.
After the main force of Malazans entered the city, the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.
Note: During Gesler's squad's attack on two
Kenryll'ah demon princes
,
Stormy
was described as being flanked by two heavies, Saltlick and Shortnose, and Saltlick's arm was broken in the fight.
But Saltlick belonged to Urb's squad, not Stormy's, and was fighting elsewhere. This appears to be an error and the text should have instead referred to either
Flashwit
or
Mayfly
, Stormy's actual heavies.
In
Dust of Dreams
(Information needed)
Spoiler warning
:
The following section contains significant plot details about Saltlick.
In
The Crippled God
He fell defending the body of the
Fallen One
against
Kolansii
infantry. A spear ripped through his throat.
Significant plot details  end here.

======================================================================
PAGE: Sands
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Sands
======================================================================

Sands
was a
marine
, a
sapper
, and a minor
mage
of the
8th Legion
's 9th Company in the
Malaz 14th Army
.  He was assigned to
Gesler
's 5th squad.
In
House of Chains
Sands was part of
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
's punitive expedition against the
Army of the Apocalypse
.  On the road from
Aren
to
Raraku
, he and
Tavos Pond
helped Gesler inspect the entrants chosen for the 9th Company
Scorpion
fight.
He was likely either the Holder or Trainer for the 5th squad's entrant,
Clawmaster
.
After the
Battle of Raraku
, Lieutenant
Ranal
raced after a group of
Leoman
's escaping men with his squads in tow.  Gesler's squad became separated from the others and was soon charged on horseback by the
Tiste Liosan
,
Jorrude
, and his men.  Gesler ordered Sands to fire a
Cusser
at the eerie warriors using the modified
Crossbow
copied from
Fiddler
's own.  Sands nervously fired the untested weapon whose explosion caused the entire hill to lift beneath them.  The charge was stopped, but
Stormy
soon had his hands around Sands' throat.
In
The Bonehunters
The 14th Army followed Leoman and the Army of the Apocalypse westward towards
Y'Ghatan
after the Battle of Raraku. Adjunct Tavore wanted to send some of her people ahead to reach the city first, so she chose Gesler's squad to accompany
Quick Ben
and
Kalam Mekhar
.  The group travelled via the
Imperial Warren
, but due to the problems with the Warrens travel was difficult and confusing.  When the group realised something was following them, Sands shakily announced whatever it was had come from
Chaos
.
The sudden appearance of at least a dozen
K'Chain Che'Malle
Skykeeps
in the air above led Quick Ben to immediately cancel the plan.  He brought the group back to the Malazan world to report the news to the Adjunct.
Adjunct Tavore launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by breaching the city's walls with sappers.  First into the city were the Malazan marines, followed quickly by the
Heavy infantry
. Barely a street in and fearing an ambush, Gesler sent Sands back to bring up
Tugg
's heavies,
Moak
's
Medium infantry
, and
Thom Tissy
's sappers.  The resulting battle was a disaster with Tissy's untrained sappers accidentally killing Moak's entire squad as well as themselves.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap.  The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. Sands fled the flames along with a mixed group of survivors from Gesler's, Tugg's,
Fiddler
's, and
Hellian
's, squads.
Sands was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city.  They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
.
Unaware that any had survived, the 14th Army made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
.
Faradan Sort
and
Sinn
remained behind and discovered the survivors as they crawled from the wreckage.
Sands and the others made the long march west, finally catching up to the army on the coast.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress
Laseen
at
Malaz City
and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Gesler and Fiddler's squads remained together and at first had no problem remaining hidden from enemy soldiers.
But the Letherii soon became aware of the enemy operating in their territory. Only
Corabb's
impossible luck saved them from a clever ambush in the forest when he accidentally flushed out a deer that immediately fell with twenty arrows in it. The Malazans quickly turned the attack with
sharpers
until the Letherii unveiled their sorcery of grey chaotic fire.
Sands was engulfed in a wave of sorcery as he charged forward, and his scream was quickly cut short as he vanished, taking his share of the squad's munitions with him. Fiddler fired a cusser into the trees above the mage killing him and shredding a score of enemy soldiers. After the Malazans escaped, Fiddler described the sorcery that took Sands as a broken gate that "chews up whoever goes through it." Bottle agreed, saying the mage had used some kind of
Hold
magic and lost control as
Chaos
took over. The mage who had killed Sands had himself been screaming as the spell took effect.

======================================================================
PAGE: Scant
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Scant
======================================================================

Scant
was a
heavy
of the
8th Legion
's 9th Company in the
Malaz 14th Army
. He likely belonged to either
Sergeant
Sobelone
's or Sergeant
Tugg
's squad.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Battle of Raraku
,
Leoman
led the
Army of the Apocalypse
westward to
Y'Ghatan
and the 14th Army followed. Adjunct Tavore launched the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
by sending the army's
sappers
to breach the city's wall under the cover of night. First into the city were the Malazan
marines
, followed quickly by the heavy and
medium infantry
. Once inside the city, the Malazans immediately came under heavy attack by hidden swordsmen and archers. Both Sergeants Sobelone and Tugg were killed.
When enough Malazans were engaged in street fighting inside the city, Leoman sprung his trap. The city's olive oil-soaked buildings were set alight and the streets quickly became an inferno. Scant fled the flames along with a mixed group of survivors from Sobelone's, Tugg's,
Fiddler
's,
Hellian
's, and
Gesler
's squads. After another attack by Leoman's fanatics, Scant and
Balgrid
corralled a grievously wounded
Tavos Pond
and guided him to safety. Scant pushed the
mage
's dangling eye back into its socket and wrapped his head in cloth.
Scant was among the small group of soldiers who survived Y'Ghatan by tunneling their way out from under the city.  They spent three days crawling on their hands and knees through the dark led by
Bottle
and his
rat
.
Unaware that any had survived, the 14th Army made haste for the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and escape the
Bluetongue Plague
ravaging
Seven Cities
.
Faradan Sort
and
Sinn
remained behind and discovered the survivors as they crawled from the wreckage.
Captain
Sort reorganised the shattered soldiers, promoting
Urb
to sergeant and placing Scant in his newly created 13th squad.
The remaining officers chose
Masan Gilani
to take the group's one remaining horse and try to catch up to the 14th Army. Gilani promised Saltlick her prized hook-blade should she not return. When Scant asked why he could not have it, Gilani said it was because she did not like him.
Scant and the others made the long march west, finally catching up to the army on the coast.
Nok's fleet returned the army to
Malaz City
where the Adjunct met with Empress
Laseen
.
In
Reaper's Gale
Adjunct Tavore clashed with Empress Laseen at Malaz City and took the
Bonehunters
rogue, following the
Tiste Edur
fleet
that had ravaged
Sepik
back to
Lether
.
Tavore invaded the
Letherii Empire
, burning her
transport
vessels on the shoreline and spreading the marines in isolated pairs of squads across thirty leagues of coast. The marines moved forward into the Letherii countryside towards
Letheras
, the capital, with orders to kill Edur by night and stir the occupied Letherii into rebellion. Each squad had a
mage
responsible for hiding their presence and confusing their enemies.
Fist
Keneb
followed in their wake with six squads of marines, while Faradan Sort and
Beak
attempted to keep lines of communication open between both groups.
Scant was made a heavy in Urb's 13th squad.
Urb's squad was paired with Hellian's for the landings and the two squads remained together with
Bowl
and
Balgrid
using their magic to cover their tracks.
After defeating a troop of Edur at
Boaral Keep
they acquired mounts at Hellian's suggestion and pushed hard inland for the capital, fighting from tavern to tavern.
The two squads began taking trophies of ear and fingers and tying them to their belts.
Contrary to the Adjunct's expectations, the Letherii soldiers did not use the Malazan invasion to turn against their Edur occupiers.
When the two squads ambushed sixteen Letherii and four Edur mounted on horseback with
Crossbows
and
Moranth munitions
, the Letherii veterans recovered more quickly than expected and
Hanno
was killed.
In the aftermath, Scant washed the blood from his hands with moss and wished
Masan Gilani
had not left the 13th for
Balm
's squad. When the inebriated Hellian tried to bed a terrified Urb, Scant recommended the bed of moss at his feet as a boudoir before they were interrupted by the arrival of Faradan Sort and Beak.
As the marines neared Letheras fighting became more desperate, although Hellian earned the support of the Letherii slave and
Indebted
classes by changing tactics to slay the government officials, lawyers, and debt-holders in each village.
Fiddler and Gesler's squads joined them at a tavern a day's travel from the capital just in time for a force of hundreds of Edur to envelop the village the Malazans occupied.
The Edur were repelled by the arrival of
Badan Gruk
,
Sinter
, and
Primly
's fresh squads.
The new arrivals deferred to Fiddler's seniority, and the former
Bridgeburner
ordered the marines to hold their position in hopes they would be reinforced by Fist Keneb.
By the time Keneb's forces arrived, thousands of Edur followed in their wake, pushing the gathered Malazans towards the city where the
Imperial Brigade
awaited.
Caught between the two armies near
Kravos Hill
, the 800 remaining Malazans
were forced to huddle under Beak's protective spell when the Letherii mages cast a deadly
ritual
of
Chaos
upon them and the Edur. The spell was broken, but the hair of all those under Beak's protection turned white. The Edur abandoned the field after their allies' betrayal, and the shaken Imperial Brigade withdrew to meet Adjunct Tavore's more threatening main force as it disembarked from the
Lether River
.
Keneb marched on Letheras thinking the marines deserved to be the first to enter the capital.
After the marines found a hidden entrance beneath the wall, Urb, Hellian, Fiddler, and Gesler's squads were sent into the city to cause trouble while the remaining marines opened the city's west gate to Tavore's infantry. Hellian's squad quickly disappeared into a local tavern and Urb was tasked with finding them.
After the main force of Malazans entered the city, the City Garrison surrendered and the city fell.

PAGE: Senny
CATEGORIES: Bonehunters
URL: https://malazan.fandom.com/wiki/Senny
======================================================================

Senny
was a
heavy
in the
Malaz 14th Army
. Circumstantial evidence suggests she was in the 3rd Company of the 8th Legion under
Captain Kindly
. She was often in the company of
Hanfeno
.
In
The Bonehunters
After the
Last Siege of Y'Ghatan
, the 14th Army marched to the coast of the
Kokakal Sea
to embark on
Admiral
Nok
's ships and return to
Quon Tali
.  While waiting for their squad's turn to board, Senny and Hanfeno gathered hundreds of bird bones to turn into fetishes for their fellow
Bonehunters
.  She spoke with
Lieutenant
Pores
, remarking on
Fist
Keneb
's seeming incompetence at organising the boarding.
Nok's ships were later met off the coast of
The Horn
by the
Jakatakan Fleet
and ordered to
Malaz City
. Senny and Hanfeno were amongst those giving Commander
Exent Hadar
and his ships a 'defecating' send-off when the two fleets parted.  Captain Kindly ordered Pores to put the two on report.
At Malaz City, Kindly's troops remained on their ships in the harbour while
Adjunct
Tavore Paran
went ashore to meet Empress
Laseen
in
Mock's Hold
.  Fighting broke out on the pier between the citizens of Malaz City and the 14th soldiers guarding the Adjunct's
flagship
.  Kindly rejected Pores' request to send aid, saying he would be happy to promote Hanfeno in the Lieutenant's place while Senny took bets on whether Pores could survive swimming to shore across the shark-filled harbour.

. They saved Henar who had been down but were killed themselves in the process. The two were described as a
Nathii
woman and a
Seven Cities
man but it was unclear as to who was who.
